














































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































Bifimer naniya Yecu Kiritti bibwe Dauda, bibwe Abrahame.
Abram co te Icaku, Icaku te Yakub, Yakub te Yahuda kange Yitub ceb.
Yahuda co te Farica Kange Jera fiye Tamar wiye, Farica nyori te Hacruna. Hacarua co te Arame.
Aram co te Aminadabe, Aminadab co te Nacone, Nacon co te Calmone.
Calmon co te Buaja fiye Rahab wiye, Boaja co te Obida fiye Rut nine. Obida co te Yeece.
Yecce co te Liya Dauda, Liya Dauda co te Culemanu fiye wii Yuriya wiye.
Culemanu co te Rehobwame, Rehobwam co te Abija, Abija co te Aca.
Aca co te Yehocafa. Yehocafa co te Yorame, Yorame cote Uziya.
Uziya co te Yotame, Yotam co te Ahaze, Ahaz co te Hezekiya.
Hezekiya co te Manacca. Manacca co te Amone, nyori Amon co te Yociya.
Yociya co te Yekoniya kange yitub cebo, dong-dong fiya cuwo ci yem ci, ci yaaken kici biten Babila.
Bwiko ci yem ci, ci yaken ci biten Babila. Yekoniya co te Ceyaltiyele. Ceyaltiyele co te Zarubabele.
Zarubabel co te Abihudu. Abihudu co te Eliyakime, nimre Eliyakim co te Azuru.
Azuru co te Caduku. Caduku co te Akimu, nire Akimu co te Aliyudu.
Aliyudu co te Ali'azara, Ali'azara co te Matana. Nimre Matana co te Yakube.
Yakubu co te Yucubu bwe Maryamu wo fiye ci wiye ci bo Yecu wo ci cuwo ti ki Almaciu.
Core tau Ibrahim nin yaken ciko Dauda nineu kaltito kwob culombo naar, kange wo tau fiye yeka ciko ci yaken ki ci Babilau yaken ciko Kiritti nin, kaldo kwob culombo naar.
Bor Yecu Kiritti ko bwi nyo wo. Nece Maryamu ciya an nam Yucufu, naci nakangiri Maryamu kweri tum fer yuwa tangbe wucake.
Yucufu bwece nii cakcake, cuibo ci neco kwenduwe nuwe nobe, nyori cuiti naci nyangum kang cinen daar.
La ci kwa diker buro tiri, bibwe tomange kwama wucake cerkangu cinen mor dukume. yi coti “Yucufu bi bwe Dauda nuware tai, tum Maryamu wimwe, wori dike ci tum ciko fwereu ca fiya yuwa tangbe wucake nen.
can do bwe, mwa cuwo dencere ki Yecu, co ca fulo nubo ti fiye bwiran ker ciye.
Gwam wo an bwi na dim diker teluwe be toke nyii nii tomange, tokti ki,
“To bubya an tu fwer, naci bo bwe ciya cuwo den cero ki Imanuel” Dike dendo nungeu “Kwama wi kange bo”.
Yucufu kwenu dumbo nineu, maani na wo bwe tomange kwama yiceu, cin kuni con tu wice.
Yucufu Nyomombo wice wi co bom bwe La con co dendo Yecu.
Bwikako ci bo Yecu Baitalami biten Yahudiya ki core wo Hirudu Liyau, Kangem nob nyomka bifumer kwama bo Urcalima. Tokti ki.
“Fee wo ci bo Liya Yahudawa? nyon to bitiren cero twar, nya bo na nyi wabka.
La Liya Hiridu nuwa nyori, kwom co kambo ken kange hwam nubo Urcalima.
Hiridu mwer Liyab wabe kwama gwam kange nob mulankab nibe. me ci “kiriti a bo fe?” Cin yi co.
“ Mor Baitalami Yahudiya nyo won co dike bibei tomange kwama mulange”.
“Mo Baitalami mor biten Yahudiya mo kebo wo duwal-duwali tiber Liyab yahudiya. more mwe an fiya nii a ca Liyar tiye wo a yila nii biyuwar nobo Lomi Iciraila”.
La Hiridu cwo nob nyomka bifumer reu, yurangum Yurange, me ci “Fiyang bitiren do cerkanguwe?”.
Con twom ci Baitalami, yiciti, “Kom ya ki fuwa bwe biduware ki Lima ki Lima, no kom fiya ri, ko bou kom yiye, na mo ken nan ya nan wabco.”
Bwikako ci nuwa diker Liya yi ciye ri cin kwen ci ta nure, bitiren do wo ci to twareu yakenti ka ci ya yan titi dor luwe bwe bi duware wiye.
La ci to bitirndo ri cin bilangi ki bilankako dur.
Cin do mor luwe, nen cin to bwe bi duwareu kange nece Maryamu. cin cung bitine cin wabco. cin kwim cwaye ciye neco Lima nerek, mwinek kange lubban kange mor.
Kwama yi ci mor dukume, ciya yilare fiye Hiridu nine. yori cin yilaken bitine ciye nure kange.
Bwikako ci kweneu cin to nii tomange teluwe cerkangu Yucufu nin yi co, “Kwen tu bwe bi duwae wo kange bece cwa cu ciko biten Masare.
Kume cuwo Yucufu tu bweu kange nece u Masar. yi ken firen yinen di na nimre, wori Huridu cuiti na twalum bweu.
Cin yike fire Hiridu Bwiyati. Wo na dim diker teluwe be tokeu nyi nii tomange, “Min cuwou bi bwemi Masar”.
Hiridu to nob nyomka Bifumereu bwanten bo ker cero ri mam funer ducce, cin twomi a twalangum bi bei nabarubbe bi duwartini gwam, wo Baitalami kange buro bi dom kange ce tati coro yob yirau ciko bitine.
Fiya cuwo la dike nii tomange Irimiya toke dimme.
Cin nuwa diro kange Rama ci wiye ti kinero fir cilong-cilonge, Rahila ci wiye dor bi beiyo locer. Mani ca fiya birum nere ti wo mani.
Fiya cuwo Hiridu bwiyame, nii tomange teluwe cerkangu Yucufu nin mor dukume mansar. yi co,
Kweni tu bwe bi duwarewo kange nece yakan Iciraila, nyori niwo do dume bwetiye bwiyam”.
Yucufu kweni tu bwe bi duware kane nece cu biten Iciraila.
La ci nuwa Akilayu bi bwe Hiridu Ca liyar ti biten Yafudiya, con nuwa tai lakako firen. Bwikako kwama yi co ker mor dukume, cin tiyangum biten Galili.
Yiken fiye kange ci cuwo ti ki Nazaret wo na dim dike ci toki nyii nob tomange ki, “Ciya cuwo co ki bwe nazare re.
Kume ni wo Yuwana yu mwem kwamam tiyeu yau ne fulen ker kwama ro ti.
Ko yiloten wori, liyar do lo kwama dadom.
won co wo nii dukume kaya tok kerce reu, “Dir nii kanger co bi cor ti kii, toki, “ko Yuwel Teluwe nin nureceu, fuwak ceko atim.
Yuwana merum ki belle yiri teleme, bwam ki dk teak fer cer. Cari ceu, kwake kange yuiti to kiyeu.
Co rubo Urcalima kange wo Yahudiya gwam, kange bitine tinim bo kong Urduneu, ci bou ti ka bo ka tuje co wiyeu.
Na ci yuu cinen mwem kwamam caji Urdun, kambo ci tok bwira kerer ce tiyeu.
La co to Faricawa kange cadukiyawa kila cirangum ti na co yu'u cinen mwem kwamamedi co ca ciye, “Kom berin nacuwe ki mwan neu, we wer kom ko cuam funero wo au tiye.
Ko ne bituti wo a nung yila ka kume ko tiyeu.
Ku kware mor ne kume kom ki Abram te kume! be ma yi kom ti, kwama wi kibi kwan do wo a kung Abram nin bibeiti fo tetendo wuro neneu.
Na wonyeu yoti biteye dimer tiniro nan, na cori tiyowo ne bo bituti keneti, an tom co na merken mor kire.
Ma Yukumen mwem kwamam bo ki mwem, ya ciko yo laka kumekeu. Niwo bouti bui mi yeu layeki dur, woro ta ceu ma labo nan tu'u. co ca yu'u kumen mwem kwamam bo ki yuwa tangbe kwama, kange kira.
Kwele yu'u ka ceko tam kang cek, can nyinagum teneu wiyak, na murom bikateceu na yo ken binico.”
La Yecu bou biten Galili, ya caji Urdun fintange Yuwana nen, na yu'u cinen mwem kwamam.
La Yuwana mani naco kicim co, tok ti ki, mo wo ma cuiti na yu'u mwem kwamam meu, mom bou minen?”.
Yecu yila yi co a ma nyo na dim cak-cakeu gwam. Co Yuwana ciya cinene.
Buiko ci yu'u cinen mwem kwamam be di, Yecu cerum can duwo mor mwenge, La dii kwama wo cinen. La co to yuwa tangbe kwamako yirau ti docer na nagumfiye, yira yiti dorcer.
La diro kange lo kwama ceru toki, wo bi bwemi ma cui cuiyeu, ma nuwa luma cek ti.
La yuwa tangbek kwamako tu Yecu yaken ciko mor yere na bwekelkele na cuwaco.
Bwiko co yi yim Ngakem kakuko kwini na'ar kumeu kwini na'ar di wura tam co.
Nii cuwa kako bou cinen yico ki, “No mo bibwe kwamari yi tero wo ayilam cari”.
Yecu yila yic mulagum mulange, Nii mani a dwiti ki cari ki kwace ce kange ker kwamar.
La bwekelkele to co yaken ciko mor cinan lor wucakeu. La kung ken co dor ku waber.
La yii co ki “No mo bibwe kwama ri, mwou bitine wori mulangum-mulange, ki “Can yi bibei tomange ce wucakeu na cer nen” La ci an kungum nen dii mor kani ciye. be na mo kware na mwek ter”.
Yecu yi ten co mulangum mulange mani mwa cuwa teluwe mwe kwama ti ko.
Tak, di Bwekelkele tu co kungken co bang ko wo cwem-cwemeu, La nung cenen Liyar do kaleweu gwam kange duktanka ciye ko.
La yico ki dike wo gwam man neken nen no mon cung cunge mo wab yeri.
La Yecu yico ki “kubom fou bwekelkele be mulangum mulange, Wab ka teluwe mwe kwama co win.
La bwekelkele dobco, La wo bibei tomange wucakeu bou cinen (wabco).
La Yecu nuwa cin tam Yuwanari, con cerum yilan ken Galili.
Co dubom Najaret cin yaken Kafanahum, wuro knog caji Galiliyeu, yii ka bitinek Jebulun Kange naftali.
wo ma nye na dim kero Icaya nii dukume tokeu.
biten Jebulune biten Nabtali wo kong Cajiyeu, kange dinge caji Urdun neu, Galili nob kumtacili.
Nubo wuro yim kumtacili yeu, cin to filanko dur, la buro yim wi fiyeceu, knage kakulok bware keu, dor cir fiya filanko ti kweni.
La fiyaco di Yecu yoten fulonka ker kwama ro, ko yolaten wori liyaro loh Kwama biyeken bidom.”
co yakenti knog caji Galili, con to yitob butib yob, cimon wo co tiki Bitru, kange Andrawu yii ce mer biliyar ti mor caji, cin nobtaka jingeb.
Yecu yii ci, kom bou ko buang menten, an yo ka ta men nob.
Dang jang ci dubom liyar cero cin buang ten co.
La Yecu dubom wi yaken tiri con to ten yitobbo kange ci yob, Yakubu bi bwe Jabali knage Yuwana yii ce, ci yim mor nabire mwenge kange jabal Tee ciye yulang biliyar ceroti.
Con co ci dang jang cin dubom nabire mwengeu kange jabali tee ciye, cim bwang ten co.
Yecu kentangum Galili gwam, merang cinen ti mor bikur waber, tok fulen ker liyar kwamaro ti twa'a mwanti tiire ti gwam kange nubo nuwabo lumau.
La fulen kere ro dor cereu yake kale mor nubo ciriya, co nubo co ci bou cinen ki nubo wo kalati ki wang ki wang kange kwirom bwi kange buro kelkelibo o cinen ti bwiyeu, kange nob juibe, kange nubo kani kange nani bwiyarangumeu, Yecu twm ci.
Nubo nawo kila kilau bwang cinen ten Galili kange dika foli kange Urcalima kange biten Yahudiya, yaken ciko dinge Urdun neu.
Kambo Yecu to mwerkang ka nubo ducceri kwiken dor bang-er. La cin yikenwi, nob bwankacebo bou cinen.
Wumom mor nerer ciro takri to merang cinen.
Bi bwiyer kiniwo bwini na yuwa tangbeceu nyori liyar kwama ki cii.
Bibwiyer kiniwo kibwatummeu, wori ciyatin macinen dangnee.
Bibwiyer ki nubo wo ki kunne wori kwalito dorbitinero ki cii.
Biwiyer ki nub wurab kange dulo mwe wucakke wori atin bwam ki cii.
Bibwiyer ki nub cika bwinib wori, atinci bwinicito.
Bibwiyer ki nubo nero wucakkeu, wori ciyen to kwama.
Bibwiyer ki nubo ki fuwer nerereu, wori a cociki bi biylo kwama.
bibwiyer ki nubo wuro cii ne cii dotangeti ker caccaker, liyar kwama ki cii.
Bibwiyer ki kom no nubo to komtiri, yila cii ne kom dotange ti ka kaa cii kwakomti kiner kan-nge bi kulentito bwir wo cuwer keceu, kermin.
Kom ma bilangtum bo man ki dii kau, wori Bitininge kumeu na dur dii kwama. Nan wo nubo ne bibei tomange dotange biro yii kaale na nyime komeu.
Kom mam dor bitinerembo cano mambo lem lumacekori, bi'amanyi na yilau cuko tak? mani ani yilamti kinan'ngen tak dila atin cutan wi na fuwarangum kina nubek.
Kom filang dor bitinero kowo cinar loro tom bidukleu mani yurangek.
Nubo mani kwer talkire tire dokken mor bulene, nyori ca kunnyii cayo fiye tikacek nane nubo luweu filang.
No nyori filang kume k acera kabum nubem ciya tom yorak na ngenek kumekotiyeu naci caklang tee kume wo dii kwama.
Km kware komki mabou nan bubam werfun nobto mangebo. ma boubo nan bubamci Dila nan dimci.
Wori bilenker miyi komti, diko kange bitineu an dim dila kiker biduwar kakaa denka win wo mani dimti mor bolang atin dim dikero kang.
Nawori niwo kimwo duwal duwale mor werfunen wonine kakaa ci merang kangum ciya manyeri, aciioco nawo duwal-duwale mor liyar kwamar.
Lari miyi komti miki “cawo-cawo cakcake kumeu tano labo cakcake nob mulangkab kange faricawbori, mani kakadokanti liyar kwamareu.
Kom nuwa kam inyi nubo nan duweu, kom taide dor, cano wo twaldoreri cikino cito warka.
La min yi kom ti woma funer kange keceri, kino mor cito warka. woyi kece, mun nifiro bwireri! cikino mor cito doka mor kirak kwamak.
Nawo nyori mwane funer nerer ti. tanyi landi kwabi kemwe wiki kwomka dorek kange mori,
Dubom luman nerok kabum tan nyi lanem, yaa yam mwem. ki kabana, fuwang kangum kange kemwe na nyi me nabou na ne funer nerer mwero.
Maa yuelka kange nii kiyangnye mwe kambo mudor nurer yaa kabum bolangem, ka nii kiyange mwe neken nen nii bolange nin nibolange an neken nen nii tomange ciyatin merkennen furcina.
Bilinker mi yinenti, mani mwa certi wi firen dila mwatin yati kemero ci bwang mwenten tieu.
Kom nuwa toki mare buraka.
Dila miyi komti, tona niwo to nawi ye, ki dilanka nuwa keri, cin kweri cin mam buroka kange co mor nerece.
Ca no nuwa me cacciyoro an dok nen kottankari, kurangum co, minangwi fiye muwiyeu. La diker win mor ayak cam, ca merbo curen buyet mwero gwam mor kira kwamak.
Kakaa kom mweko cacciyero tano atin atim dok nen kottang kari, mwattumco miranwi fiye muwiyeu. wori in La diker win mor a yakcam, kange merka buye mweko gwam kirak kwama.
Yilam to ki niwo ywa wice ri, a neco bifumer nyaka kangeko.
Dila miyi komti tano wo ywa wiceri, cano nobo dor kangka diker kayakardi, cin yilam kico ni burokak.
Kom nuwa ten cin yi ki nubo burombo nan duwoo kom werde weri cwerke, dila kwama werka kumeko kwamanin.
Dila miyi kom ti komti kom werde weri di kwamaka wori Nkunjala kwama;
kakaa kange dorbitiner fititim nanice, kakaa Wurcalima, wori biten liya dur.
Ca bu nano ka werweri ki dor kumerdi, la mani ka dolti kom yilam ki yiri duwekume fuwoje kakaa fije.
Dila Ker kumero a yilam NYO Nyo, nonindi 'Nyonin, nyonin. Cano dikero cumweri, kino bwirkonin.
Kom nuwa toki ki, Nuwe nyii nue nundo tak nyii nunne.
Dila miyi komti kom mare Kwobkangka kange niwo na bwireu, nyiyoco nyeu, no cii malicom dan-nge cattiyereri, kom yilam cinen wineu ken.
No ni kannge wii a yakenti ki kiyange kume kabum boulangem meriwori naci yo belle kueri kom netten nii wo lalan kumeko.
Cano ni dokkom yam nako kwininugri kom ya kannyace yob.
Komne nii wo mekomeu, tak kom kware niwo do naan ti kumeneu.
Kom nuwa dike tokeu, mwan cii ni bidome mweu mwanko ni kiye mweu.
Dila min yi kom ti kom cii nob kiyeb kume bo, kom kwob nubo nekom dotannge tiye nin dilo kom ma nubowuri, cil komenin bibuyer, komma nubo wo ko kom tiyeu nin dikoro ken.
Naweu nakom yilam bibiyo lo tekume wo dikwamau. wori dok kakuko wennii bwirninti kannge nii ken twom wucakke kannge nii maakenin mwom dikwamati.
Wori cano kom ki cwi nubowuri cwikom tiyeri, nyii dikedde kom fiya? kebonyo nob yoka doreko matiya?
Kume keneu tano kom yarum ka 'Kebkumebri, yekamani la tangece? kobonyo nubo nyombo kwamau matiya?
Dila naweu nyi lam nyo kom yilam cikocok nawo tekumu wodiyeu.
Kom yilam yiber dover ko mare luma kume ko kabum nubem be naci tokom, no kom ma nyori, mani ka fiya cuneti fiye tee kume wo dii kwama wiyeu.
La naweu, no kama luma tiri kom cure cume kambo nubo bwirko mati ku wabe kannge dor nurereu wori na nubo caklang ci. Bilinker miyi kmo ti cin fiyam nyii diker cero.
La tano kama luma tiri kam kume moutkeu anyomde dike kango cattiyero matiyeu.
Wori na lumake meko na yilam yurangum yurannge. Tee kume wuro to dikeroti yuragum yurangeu, atin makumen cuner.
Tano kmbo ka kwob diloti takeri, kom yilam de na nubo bwirko, wori ci cwikwoka diloti timotiye ku wabece kannge cuga nurek tak, wori na nubo toci. bilenker miyi kom ti cinn fiyam cuner ceko fou kale.
La tano kom kakwob dilotiri, kom doken mor kuwe. Kom nungum nyiloko, kom kwobdilo Tee kume wo yurangum yurange an nekom cuner kumero.
Ca no ka kwob dilotiri, kom libride diker manki nagenneu. nawo nubo nyombo kwama matiyeu. wori kwanererceu ciyatin cuwa tuuki keticro dukceu.
Na weu ko yilamde naci wo Tee kume nyimoum bwini kumero kikinning nanyime kom kenco.
Na wori kom kwobdilo nawo Tee bewo dii kwamau, ane den mwero dur wucak.
Liyar mwero a dou ner nuber.
Ne nyo carto na dume ce kume -kume.
Dob Nyinen bwirang kert nyero. nawo nyi dob nubowo ma yinentiyeu.
Yare kinya Fiye cuwaka, dila cok nyo nii bwir konin (kanng Liyar kannge bikom liyaret kange duktanka ka na mwe diri diri ati nyo).
Wori no kom dob nubori bwira kerer cirori, Tee kume wo dii kwamau an dobkumen ken.
Ca no ka dobbo nubonen bwirang keretinin cirori Tee kume mani a dob kumen ti.
Nyotak, no kama nyak tiri, kom yilam kitikob na nuwoma mwamangtu tiye kambo nubo bwirko matiyeu, wori ci kwuob kang yirom cimboti wori naci dannyi kabum nubem mwincimen Nyak ti. Bilenker miyi kom ti ci fiyam cuner cero.
Dilacano kom ma Nyak tiri kom beltu nuwan der kom nirum tikob kumebo.
La nanubo nyumde kom ma Nyak ti, lakan Tee kume wo to dikero kom matiyeu yurangumeu ati makumen.
Kom mwerde dor kumero nii cuweka for dor bitinet, fiye kerkere kange cnkume a kanngum tiyeu, fiye nob kubbo bani werti do kuumme.
Nyiyoco Nyeu, kom mwer dor kumer kange nii cuwaka firen dii kwama fiye kerkere kannge cankume mani yeu. nawo a kanngum tiye fiye tak nuu kuyee mani werti na kumme.
Fiye cuweka mweu wiyeu ner mwero ki nowi ken.
Nuweu co talkire bwiyeu. Nawori cno nuwemweu yorari, bwiyo kwarub dimki filang.
la cano nuwemweu dikero kendi bwiyo kwarub dimki kumtacile.
Nii mani bwiya bwnagten, Tee yobe La catin ciya wi ci ko win mani nyori can ciya kanyenin win ci cuyekangum wiceu.

Nyori ca no kom bwirembo, ko yumum kambo kane bibiyo lokume lumako tiye, kambo Tee kume diyeu a ne kom dikero kentiye.
Na woro di gwamra dikero kom ci ti nubo amakume neu, kom macinen ken.
Kom doken nure wo dwaldwaleu, wori nure buareu kuya in nurewo bwaibo doka nob dokabo moreceu ci kila kabo.

wo ne win more bi duwartini buru kwel mwenge yibe nano ki den ni bwangkake ri, bilenke mi yi komti mani a le cuner cero ti”.

wori co dike bwi mi yici keroti ki dangke. To na ci ti toi ri mani ciya toti, tano citi nuwei ri ma ciya nuwati kaka nyimom.

Kom nuwa dangke niwo ya fi fikeu.
No kangumbo fulen liyar kwamar nyombe ri, nii bi cirene an bou bo yuwom dike ci finer cereu. won co dumbo ci fi nureu.
W ci fi fiye bitine ki terentiye, co niwo nuwa kero ri yuwa wulom-wulom ki for neret.

mor nee kwabanka digero bwir cirutiye, twal ka duwe, kayaka, Bwirangtum, kwii warkere cwerke kange tor kanganka.

La Yecu yila ten mor bikur waber la nikange wo Yecu kanko nom-nokeu.

La con to ciki funer, nercero kayam kaya kibi kwan duwer cin la co yi nii co, tarken kanmweko la can tarken kance kori la Yecu tamco.
La faricawa ceri wulom-wulom yaken fiye nubo lo Hiridu wiyeu la tokkangum nure wo ciya twalum co tiyeu.
La Yecu kange bibei tomange ceu ci yaken koncaci la nubo kila bwang cinenten, tabti Galili kange Yahudiya.
Tabti Urcalima kange Edom kab kange Urdun kange kentankako Tayau kange Cido. La ci nuwa dikco matiyeri nubo kila bou cimen.
La ci mwe bibei tomangeb ceu a docimen nabire mwenge biduware a timtiye worinubo kila, kati yilo ci kwenan cinenten.
Con too nubo kila kila, wo nubo twirau doti kawo naci kem bwiciu.
No na kelkelibo tocori ciki cung cung kaaco ci kwa kiyange kibi kwan ciki mo bi bwe kwama.
La con yi cikibi kwan ci a dok re nubo a nyomom co.
La con kwiken dor banged, la con co nubo co cui tiyeu, co ciya cinen.
con cokum kwob cilombo yobeu (con co cibibei tomange) buro a yiti kange ceu, naco twom ci naci tok fulen kereroti.
Con ne ci bikwan kerer wo ci a cokum kelkelibotiyeu.
Con cokum nubo kwob cilombo yob, won caminu co ne co dendo Bitru.
Yakubu bi bwe Jabadi kange Yuwana yii Yakubu, wo ca ne ci dendo Buwanarji no co bibei kunye.
Kange Andirawu, kange Filibu, Kange Batilomi, Kange Matta, Kange Toma, Kange Yakubbu bibwe Alfa, Tadawu Caminu bwekananiya.
Kange Yafuda ikariyoti wo a miye co tiyeu.
La con doken mor luwe nubo kila kicangeu yila bourengu mwerti wo dokci ci cabo cariye.
Nubo lo ce nuwa nyori, co ci ceru we naci tamco, ci tokti ciki, mani mor dume nece.
Nob mulankabo yirau Urcalimau, ki ba'al zabu kwiken dor cere, kibi kwan liya kelkelir co cokan kelkelib tiye.
Yecu cou ci fiye co wiye, la yici dangeke ki, bwe kelkele a cok bwe kelkele nyi?
La nyo na liyar an tikan bwiciri, liyardo co manki tika.
No na luwe yalkan bwiti ciyeri luwe co mani a tii ti.
La no bwekelkele kung dor ceri nin ten yalkangum ri mani a titi tak, ciile ceu beken.
Nii mani a doti lo nibi kibi kwan na yem kulen do mor luweu, kebo kiwo ca bwabangum na'a ni bikwaneu. na nimre co yem kulendo mor luwe ceu.
Kibi com maa yikomti bwiranker bibe ifire maneu an to tabum ciko, kange ketito bwirko wo ci tokkeu.
Nii wo na tok kero bwir dor yuwa tangbaek kwamereri, mani a fiya tabkati, la mani a ma bwirangkero ti tak bak ni bak.
Yecu tok wori ciyico tiki con wiki yuwa kelkelek.
La neece kange yitub cebo bou tirangum kale, lacin two cimen ki nyiyal co a bou.
Nubo mwerum kentangum co, coci yico ker kinee mwe kange yitub mwebo wo fo kale, ci donenti.
La cin karcimen we nemi kange yitub mibo?
La yila con to nubo yii kentangum ceuri, yici ki nemi wo kange yitub mifo foo.
Niwo ma dike kwama cuitiyerii ni co yim, kange kor-yami kange nemi.
La con ter merankako kong caji. nubo kilakila mwrum wi kentangum co, ta con doken mor nabire menge mor caji con yiken morcer. Nubo mwerum wiyeu yim ciye dukle kong caji.
La co merang cinen dikero ducce ki dangke, mor merangka ceko con yiki.
Ko to cinen nii fike kange yaken fik dumek.
Co mor waka dumek ri, kangem dumembo yarangti mure bilibeteni bon mirangum.
kangembo yarangken fiye ki tetten, bitine cuwabo.
La kakuko kwiuri cin comam, wori ci manki niye niye ken cin kwicim.
kangembo cin yarken mor cuiwakkek ci dwiyang ken tiwi la cuiwakko cakkangum ci, cimabo nuni.
Kangem dumebbo yarangken bitine ken kwen tuu duyangi ma nuni kangembo bilako kwini taar, kangem bo kwini nukkun, kangembo kwini kwob.
La yi ci niwo ki tu'u nuwakakeri anuwa.
La Yecu ki kwaceri, nubo bi dom knge ceu kange kwob cilombo yobeu, cin me co diker dangke wo nung tiyeu.

wori to ka ki nuwe cin tom, laci nyombo, nuwakako cin nuwam fire ci bo, kati ci yilamri tabcinen bwirangkeu.

ciyeu la ci manki niti, manki bikwan, no dotange kange bune bou ki kero wori can candowo cin an yarum.

Nii kitu'u anuwakau anuwa.

wori nii ki dikereu ki yok cimenten yok, nii man cikeu an yom cinen na yok nii cikeu nenten.

Bitineu kibwici kinem cari nyo, kii kako co kabako.

Na nun nyincine, no na fii cori co bi duwareu mor nuni dor bitinereu.

Liya Hiridu nuwa nyo den Yecu ylam nyomom nyome nubo nin gwam. kangem bo yiti ki Yuhana nii yumweti kweni tuwe co diker bwi ci maran nagen nyomankako wo ticinene.
Kangem bo yiti ki Iliya nyo na wo kangem yiti ki win mor toka dukume
Hiridu nuwa wori con yiki Yuwana wo ma mwotum dore co kwene ka?
Hiridu doki a ta Yuhana na merken fucina ki ker Hirodiya (wii Filibu yice). Na co nam co.
Wori Yuwana yi Hiridu ki dabo ca na wi yice.
La Hirodiya tii ner na co twalum Yuwana dila mabo.
Nori Hiridu nuwa Tai Yuwanati con Nyomom Yuwana nii wucakke take cakcak. Hiridu ciya bo knage dikero a fiya Yuwana. na co nuwa fulen kerero Yuwana toktiyeu funer cero kweni kange nyo ki furwor neret coki cuware tuu nuka ceke.
La hirodiya fiya da can ma diker co cwi makatiyeu kakuk boka ceko kentangu Hiridu co cika, nubbo durko ma mangenti mor liyare ceu, kange nubo durtinimbo mor Galili.
Bubiya Hiridu yelyilako yori Hiridu kange fabubcebo nen Liya yi bubiya ca tok diker co cwitiyeu man nenen.
Con ner cinen ki ye co cwitiye, bwen Liyar cerdi can biyeri co nen co.
Ceri yaken ya me nece “Ye ma yi coti ca ne yere?” La ki dor Yuwana nii yuka mwem me.
Bubiya wo yilau wulom mor kuwe nubo mwerum wiye ki a neco dor Yuwana nii yuka mwemek mor fantilange.
Ko liya kambo ken, co manki diker maka kweri co tum nor kabum nob nangeneb ceb.
Liya twom nii bwa dak tiye ca ya ca bo cinen ki dor Yuawanako.
Nii bwa dak tiye ya matuii dor Yuawana ro, furcuna nyou fantilan bo ne bubiya, bubiya ya nee nece.
Bibei tomange ci nuwa Nyori yatu bilendo fwerum tuwe.

La cin ceri mor nabire mwenge ki bwitici.
Nubo dutce tom ci yaken ti, cin yomom ci, la ci cerangum cinan loronen ka cwak, ci yulum ci.

me ci ki cwen carito nyi kom cike? kom ya, ya kom tou “ya ci touri chwendo nung kange jinge yob”.

Co to ci, ci nuwa dotange ti, yuwako yuwamci yam. keno lam nar na kwomce ce la con bo fiye ci wiye, yakenti dor mwenger, co citi na co cuken kabum cem.
Di cin to co yakenti dor mwenger la ci kwati keno kelkeliri, cin kwa kiyange.
Gwam ciye cin tomco, tai to tam ci. can nawo con tok ker kange ci coki, kom ma bi kwan neret kom nuware tai.
Doken mor nabire mwenge wari kange ci, la Yuwako tam figlanka ciyeko, diker nyomankar tam ci kambo kem.
Ci ynombo ker cwen do. Nyori ner ciyero kiyabo.

Wori Canyi lan ki dur kabuni Te-luwe. Mani co no mwem bi tuittuibti kaka diker no karo kwam kwame, Catin din ki yiwa tangbe ko wucakeu mor fwiye nece.
Naniyak Iciraila ko duce wo a yila cuko Teluwe kwama Cenen.
Can ya kabum Teluwe mo yu wa tangbo kange bikwan Iliyak, Na yilau ki ner tebembo bibeyo nen kange wo bongi nyeu na ya mor nyomka cak-cake -na ci Ywel te luwe nin nubo wo ci cok cineneu.”
Zakariya yi Bwetanange wucake “Ma nyom dike wo nyi? wori min cele ri wimi coro kilam”.
Nii tomangeu wucakeu Ciya yicoki “Mo Jibrai'lu, wo tire kabum kwamau. Cin tomu ye nami yinen ker, nan bo mwen ki kero lomlome.
La to! Mwan yilam cōk, mani mwa dol tokka kere ti, dila diya dikero buro dimmeri ntimade. Wori mwi nebo bilenker ker miro nin, wo a diiti ki kwama dong-donge
La nubo ningtang Zakariya ti. Cin nyimangi wori cinti lenger mor bikur waber.
Dila ki kwa'ma ci ceruweri, dolbo yici ker. La ciin nyimom ki cin to dukum ki kwamawo ci mor bikur-wabereu. La cin nungkancinen ti ki kank worimani citok ker ti.
La yilam kambo kumeni nanger cero cume ri, cin cu lo co.
Kambo kume ni wo cumeri, wice Alicabatu tum fwer la cin yu rangum dorceri na cuwako nunge ce. Cin yiki,
“Wo lo diker kwama mamene kambo ci toye ki corciniyeu, naci tum kwenduwe miu ka nobe.
Ki ciwako nukkune, kwama tom nii tomange wuccake Jibrailu mor Cinanlor Galili ci coti ki Nazaret,
bubiya nin wo cine ken nii kange wo den cero Yucufu, wo naniyak Dauda, la bubiya dendo Maryamu.
Cin bow Cinenri ciki, “A Ysrumnen, mo wo fiya cini ducce! Teluwe wi kange mo”.
La cin kulongum duce, ki kercero la cin kwabi, ya rume ye wo.
Bwe tomange wuccake yicoki, “Cuware tai, Maryamu, wori mwin fiya cini kwama nin.
To, mwan tu fwed ri na mwi bo bwe. Mwa cun den cero 'Yecu'.
Can yilam nii dur la ci cuu ki Bibwe nii dur re. Teluwe kwama atin ne co kuti le liyare Tekwace Dauda.
Can ma liyar dor lo Yakubu diiri, Liyar cero manki dika”.
Maryamu me bibwetomange wuccake ki; “Dike wo a bwinyi la mi nyumumbo nii na bare wiyeu?”
Bibwe tomange kwaama ciya ri yi co ki, “Yuwa tangba kwamako an bow mwinen, ri bi kwan nii dur reu atin bow dor mwer. La wucakke wo mwi bo tiyeu a coki Bibwe kwama.
To, na niya mweko Alicabatu tu fwer ki ciraka ceko. Wo co cuwiyak ceko mukkune, co wo no ci cuoti ki combilomeu.
Di kero kange mani wo mani a mati kabum kwama”.
Maryamu yi ki, “To, min bubiya canga kwama. A yila men na tomange meu”. Dila bwe tomange kwama dob co.
Dila Maryamu kweni ki kume tini co wulom wulom yaken mor bi ten kongtini, yaken bi ten Yahuda.
Ciin yaken mor luwe Zakariya ri cin yarum Alicabatu.
Yilam kambo Alicabatu nuwa yarume Maryamu ri bwe mor fwe ce mokangi la Alicabatu diim ki yuwa tangbako wucake.
Ciin kung dir cero kibi kwan ciki, “Mwin nii bi bwiyere mor natube, ri nii bwiyere bwe wo mor fwiye meu.
Ye bwi wo fiya yenye, la ne Te luwe mi a bou ti mi nene?
La ta kambo diir yaru mer mwero bou tu miyeri bwe fwe.
Nii bi bwiyere co nawiye wo ne bilenke ki digero wo ciyi co fiye kwama wiye atin dii me.
Maryamu yiki “Dume miu caklang Te luwe
re, yuwa tangba miu bilangi kwama nii cyer yerenin.
Wori cin to cukka dorek bubiya canga ce. La to, nawo kange kab kaltini gwam a co yeki nii bi bwiyere.
Wori co, wo nii bi kwaneu, ma men digero dur, la den cero wucak.
Jire duwe ceu tii nyo kal ya ciko kaleu ki buro wo nuwa taicero tiyeu.
Cin nung bi kwancero ki kank cek, cin yalum buro ki kunka duwek keu ki dike ci kwati neer cere.
Cin cukkangum bi bei liyabbe dor kutile cero nin, la cin kungum nob fuebbo.
Cin cam ki nob wurabbo ki diketi no ken, dila nubo cuwe cuweu cin yoken ci kang kwicer.
Cin ne canga ce Iciraila tikali, nyori naci kwabi naci nung jire duwe
(Nawo ci yi tebbe beu) ciyi Ibrahim kange naniyak ceke diri.
Maryamu yi kange Alicabatu cuyako ta'ar ri cin yilaken lo co.
La kwama bou na Alicabatu a bom bwi bwece, la cin bou bwe bwayile.
Nubo bi dom kange ca kange na niyak ceko nuwa ki kwama nung cinen Jire duwe ce durko, la cin bilangi kange co.
La yilam ki diye naruberi cin bow naci mwatum lar bwero. Ciikin cuom co “Zakariya”, na den te cero.
Dila neele ciya ki o, onga. “A cuoco ki Yuwana”
Cin yicoki, “Nii kange man mor naniya kumek wo cico tiki dendo we”.
Cin nung tece ninki kang kambo ci cuiti naci ne co dendeu.
Tece me ci ya neco ter mulankar la cin mulangi, “Den cero Yohanna”. Cin nyimangi gwam dor dikero wo.
Dangjang dangjang nyi ceu wumom ri la biyen cero fiya cyer ka. cin tok ker la cin cak lang kwama.
Taito bou dor nubo gwam wo yim Cunga cekeu. Kerowo yalati gwam mor biten kongni Yahuda.
Nubo gwam wo nuwa ri, yoken mor nere ce, tokti ki “La ye bwewo a yila tiye?” La kang Te luwe ko wi kange co.
Tece Zakariya diim ki yuwa tangbe ko wuccake la tok ker dukumer, ki
“Caklanka fiye Teluwe wiye, kwama Iciraila, cin bow naci ma tikali la cinma nob cebo nin cerka.
Cin kung binek cume fuloka lo canga ce Dauda,
(nawo ci tokki nyi nob tomange ceu kwattiye),
fuloka nob kiyeb beu kange nubo wo kwerbo nyeu.
Can ma wuro naci nung, tebbe bo nin jire duwe ri la naci kwa nor cero wucak keu,
weri wo ci yii tebo Ibrahim.
Cii weri naci nebo co kambo ci cokum bo kange nob kiyeb bekeri, nabi bwangci nenten kibi kwan neret
mor wucakke kange cak-cake kabum cem ki kumetinibeu kale we nin gwam.
O, kange mo, bwe, ciya co nen ki bwe tomange nii durre, la mwan yaken kabum tikobe Te-luwe ri na mwi ywel nure ceu, na mwi ywel nubo ki boka ceko
na ne nob cebo nyom ka fulokak ki tab ka bwirank kerer cero.
Wo an bwi wori jire duwe kwama beu duwi kabo, wo kercer di filango ceru dii yeu atin bou na tikangbo,
na ne filang ki nubo wo yim kumta cilenen kange kakulok bwareke. Ca tin ma wuro na bwangten ki nabe ko mor nure lima nereke
La bweu dwi la yilam ki bi kwan mor yuwa tangba, la ciki no mor yere na nyimde diye ci ter cerkako yanglang Iciraila.
La ki kumetini co, kaicar Augusta tung tomange cin toki ciki a kiyeu nubo gwam wo yim dor bitinereu.
Won co kiye ka kaba maneu ki kwama wo kiriyuc ma liyar ti curiya.
La nubo gwam yarangen cinanlor cer naci mulangum ki kiye kakor.
Yucufu ken kwenu Galili wo mor cinanlor Nazaret la cin yaken Yahuza, cinanlor Dauda, wo cuoti Baitalomi, wori ciki no naniyak Dauda.
Cin yaken wi naci mulangum dercero kange Maryamu wo ci bob beu la ki fwer.
La kambo ci wi ye ri, kwama lam wo ci bom bwe tiye lam.
Cii bo bwe bibare, bwe kaba ce, la cin kwomum co ki yilang ko cuwe mer la yoken co mor tokum nennem wori ci man ki fiye wi.
La nob biyuwareb bo wi cungako co ci dami ner bitibere to bi cir cero ti ki kume.
Bwe tomange Te luweu cer cinen, la duktangka Te luwek ko tebum cunga ceko, la cin dim ki tai ducce.
Dila Bwe tomange kwama yici “Ko cuware tai, wori mi bo kumen ki kero ken wo a bou hi ki fuwor nerero dur nubo nin gwame.
Duwen cin bo kimen nii fuloka mor cinan lor Dauda! Cin Kiritti Te luwe!
Wo co yirombo wo ci nekom tiye, kam fiya bweu kumon mor yilango cuwemer, yom mor tokum nennem.
Dangjang ri bwe tomange kwama kange mwer kamka dur ko dii kwa'ma caklang kwama ti ciki
“Duktanka ki kwama firen dii, rila fuwor nere a fiya tiber nubero co (Kwama) ciyacike.
La yilam kambo bi bei tomange kwama dubom ci yilaken dii lo kwamari, nob bi warebbo yi bwiti ci, “na weu ko biya Baitalami nabi to dikero wo bwiyeu, wo Teluwe nung bi neneu”
cin cu wulom-wulom wii dila cin fiya Maryamu, Yucufu kange bwe fiyerko dam mor tokume.
Kambo ci tom ceri, cin yi nubo dikero cii yi cii dor bwe fiyerko weu.
Gwam wo nuwari, ma nyimanka dor dikero nob bi yuwarebbo yi ci yeu.
Dila Maryamu ki bulangi dor digero ci nuwa gwam, la cin yoken mor nerece.
Nob bi yuwarebo yilaken ci duktangi ri ci caklank kwama ti ki dikero gwam woci nuwau kange wo ci toweu dong-dong nawo ci yi ciyeu.
Kambo kume narube dimeri, fiyaco ci biye cinen lareu cin ne co dendo Yecu, dendo bwe tomange kwama ne na nyinde cii tu fwer cereu.
Kambo kumeni wucakeu ce cumeri, na wo mor wer fun mucaro, ciin bou ki co bikur waber mor Urucalima naci neken co kwama nin.
Nawo mulangum mor werfun Te luwe “Gwam bwe kabo wo bwayileri, atin cokum co ki dimen, cina kwama ce.
La cin ma wabka nawo ci toki mor werfun Te luwe re, “nagum fe yob kakaa kalti nawurmero yab”
La Nii kange wi Urucalima wu dencero cimon ne, ni wo cak cak laci ne dor bwanka kwama. Ciki ningtan nii a bii Iciraila nin neer tiye, la yuwa kange kwamak wi kange co.
La yuwa tangbe kwamako nungcine ki mani ci bwiyati ne citom Kiritti Teeluweri nyinde.
La yuwa tangbe kwamako ya ki co mor bi kur waber. Kambo Teb bwe fiyerko Yeco bou kice, naci macinen nawo werfundo nungeu,
cin tu beu kangcek ri cin caklang kwama, ciki,
na weu dob bwe canga meu akubo ki fuwor neret Teluwa nawo mori tokeu.
La nuwe mi tom fuloka mweko,
wo mwi yweli nuwe nubo gwammer:
filang dukumek wo nubo kumta cili cee kange duktangka wo nubo lomwe Iciraila ce.
Tee ce kange nee ce ma nyimankka ki dike ci toki dorce reu.
Cimon yocinen bibwiyer, ri yi Maryamu nece ki “Nuwa Yora, bwewo cin co ki na boki yare kange kwenka nubo duce Iciraila na yirome wo ci kowe
kange kulen wo abiye ken mor nere mwetiye rila bi kwarum nerem bo kila atim ceruu”.
Nawiye tomange kwama ci cuo ti ki Anna wiwi. Cibi bwe Panuel naniya Acar. La cin duyom ki cotini duce, cin yi kange bwece coro kwini niber,
la cin nawi ye kwale coro kwini narub-cilombo na'ar. La mani ci dob mor bi kur wabe ri ci wab kwama ki ngak ngake kange dilo kume kange kakuk.
Ki kwama co dondong cin kwitau laidom kange ci, ri cin ter buka kau kwama, la cin yi nubo ningtang fuloka Urcalima kotiye ker dor bwero nin.
Kambo ci dim digero da ter cin matiye nawo mulangum mor werfun Teluwere di, cin yila keu Galili mor cinanlor ceer Nazaret.
La bwen duyom yilam kibi kwan, kange nyomka, la luma kwama wii cinen.
Ki cor teb ce bo ki yam nyo Urucalima ki duklume yabka.
Ki kwamawo ci dim coro kwabcilom bo yebeu, cin yaken tag duklumenin.
La kambo ci diim kumeni duklume gwame ri, cin ter yila kako loweu. La beu Yecu tim ce bwi mor Urucalima ri la teb cebo nyombo.
Ci kwotiri ciki no mor mwerka nube kowo ci yaken ti wari yeu. La cin ya yam kume wiine. Di cin ter doka ceko mor naniya cek kange farub cek.
Kambo ci fiya ceberi, cin yila ken mor Urucalima la cin ter doka ceko wi.
La bwiko kume taare ri cin fiyamco mor bikur waber, yim tiber nob merangkab merangci ke tiniti.
La gwam wo nuwa ce ri, ma nyimangka ki nyomka ceko kange ciyaka ceko.
Kambo ci toceri, nyimankako tamci, la nee ce yico ki ““ye bwi mwa manyo nye? To, tee mwe kange mo nyi do nen ti ki kwomka duce.” Cin yici, “Ye bwi kom doye tiye? Ko nyombo kambo mamanangen mira?”
Con yi ci, ye bwi kom do ye tiye? kom nyomba tam nyo ma nangen Temera?
Di ci nyombo dike co yi ti kange kero co toke.
La cin yaken lo kange ci mor Nazaret la ci nee ci dur ti. Nee ce yoken diker buro gwam mor nere ce.
Dila Yecu ki duwi mor nyomka kange cuwemka la cin fiya cor cini kwama nin kange nob.
Mor coro kwob cilombo nung wo liyar Tibariyuc, la Bilatu Buntu bwangtentiki Yahuda, Hiridu co liya Galili, yice Filibu liya cungako Ituriya kange Tirakonitic, la Licaniyac liya Abiliya,
ki kwama Annac kange kayafa nob wabe bo dur keu - ker kwamaro bou Yohana bibwe Zakariya nin mor yere.
Cin ya mor bitenni gwam wo cunga caji Urdun ne. Ne fulen ker yika mwenge yilokati na fiya tab ka bwiran kerer.
Nawo mulangum mor bi fumer Icaya nii tomange dukumeu, “Diro wo cuo bicor timor yere ko ywelum nure Teluwe, kom tim ki nure ceu ciyer.
Bunglunge gwam atim dim, la bangtini gwam kange dukletini atin daken, nureni nyon langi nyeu atin tiken ciyer, fiye bweyang bweyangeu atim twilangum na yilam nure,
la nubo gwami auto fuloka kwama”.
La Yohanna ji nubo bouti cinen naci yu cinen mwembeu “Kom biwei fangeb! we yi com ki kom cuwa funer wo yautiye?
Nyori, kom ne bibeyo wo daten yilaka kumeke, la ko yire dor kimero kom ki “nyin wi tee nye Ibrahim”. La mi yi komti, kwama atin kung Ibrahim nin naniya teren ti wo nin.
Wo na weu, biliyeu yom niti tiyer. La tiyo wo nebo bi tuttiyeri atin tom na merken mor kire.
Dila nubo ti meka ceko “Ye nya matiye?”
Cin ciya cinen ciki, “No kange kume wi ki belle yob ri, ca ti kangum kange nii womancike, wo ki cariyeri a mani nyo ken”.
Nob yoka doreb bou ken naci yu cinen mwembo, la cin yi co ki “Nii merangka, ye nyi matiye?
Ciin yi ci, “Ko yore kemero a cure dike ci yi kom ko yoweu”
Kangem nob kweneb me co ken ki “La nyeu? Ye nyi matiye?” Cin yi ci “Ko yore kemer nii nin kibi kwam ri, ko mwelde nii nin ker ki cuwerke. Ko bulang ki kemer cuwakek kumeko
La kambo nubo ningtang bo ka Kiritti tiye ri gwam ce ki kwai mor nere ce dor Yohanna keno co Kritti ri.
Yohanna ciya cinen gwam, “Miu, miki yu kumen bwembo ki mwem la kange wi ber wo laye bikwaner, ma labo wo ma kiwi duka ta ceko tiyeu. Ca yu kumen mwembo ki yuwa tangbe kwama kange kira.
Kwel yuka ceko kino kang cek na nyinangum tene ceu na mwerken bikate mor bini. La ca tin twim fwirito ki kirako man ki domka”.
Ki weranka duce tak, Yohanna yi nubo fulen kerero ken ti.
Kambo ci werank Hiru liya ki naka wi yi ceko Hirudiya, kange dikero bwiir tini kangem bo Hiridu maneu.
Cin cob ten ki buro gwam, ri cin kum Yohanna fucina.
La kambo nubo gwam yum mwem beri, cin yu Yecu nin mwembo ken. La ki kwama ci kwob dilo tiyeri dii kwama wumom,
Dila yuwa tangbe kwamako yirau cinen na nagumfe, la diro ceru dii kwama “Mwi bwe nere mii, mi nuwa luma mwek ti?
Ki kwamawo Yecu ter nangen cere, can lam coro kwini ta'ar. Cir bi bwe (nawoci kwabi bereu) Yucufu, bi bwe Heli,
bi bwe matat, bi bwe Lewi, bi bwe Malaki bi bwe Yanna bi bwe Yucufu.
Yucufu bi bwe Mattatiya, bibwe Amoc, bi bwe Nahum, bi bwe Idacli, bibwe Najjaya,
bibwe Ma'ata, bibwe Mattatiya, bibwe Climeya bibwe Yoceku, yo ceku bibwe Yoda
Yoda bibwe Yowana, bibwe Reca bibwe Zerubbila bibwe Ciyeltiyele, bibwe Niri
bibwe Malki, bibwe Addi, bibwe Kocama, bibwe Almadama, bibwe Er,
bibwe Yoci, bibwe Aliyeza bibwe Yorima, bibwe Matat, bibwe Lawi,
bibwe Caminu, bibwe Yahuda, bibwe Yucufu, bibwe Yohanna, bibwe Aliyakima,
bibwe Malaya, bibwe Mainana, bibwe Matata, bibwe Natan, bibwe Dauda,
bibwe Yesse, bibwe Obida, bibwe Calmon, bibwe Nacon.
bibwe Amminadab, bibwe Adimi, bibwe Arama, bibwe Hezruna, bibwe Feresa, bibwe Yahuda,
bibwe Yakubu, bibwe Icaku, bibwe Ibrahim, bibwe Tera, bibwe Nahor,
bibwe Cerug, bibwe Reyu, bibwe Feleg, bibwe Abiru, bibwe Cela.
bibwe Kainana, bibwe Arfakcada, bibwe Cem, bibwe Nuhu, bibwe Lamek,
bibwe Methucela, bibwe Anuhu, bibwe Yaret, bibwe Mahalel, bibwe Kainana,
bibwe Enoc, bibwe Citu, bibwe Adamu, bibwe Kwama.
La Yeecu dim ki Yuwa tangbe kwama, yilam firen caji Urdun la yuwa tangbe kwama ko tu co yakanciko yerak.
Fiye kume kwini na'ar bwekelkele cuwaco tiyeu. co ca diker ki kumeni co, la ni connuwa wura.
Bwekelkel yii, na mo bibwe kwamri yii tero wo a yilam cari,
Yeecu yii co, mulangum mulange “ke bo ka cari ni ama dumetiye”.
La bwekelkele kung ken Yeecu dii nung cinen liyaro kaleweu gwam.
Bwekelkele yii co, “man neken nen Bikwankero gwam kange duktanka ceko, wori cin neyen dike buri gwam, la man weken nii wo ma cuitiyeu.
Na ceu na mwan cung cunge mo wab yeri gwam ka mwe”.
La Yeecu karci nen yiico, mulangum mulange mwa wab “Teluwe kwama mwe, co ki kwace mwa- Bwangtentiye”.
So bwekelkele yakan ki Yeecu Urucalima, kung ken co diiku'u wabe la yii co na mo bi bwe kwama di yarubitine
wori mulangum mulange, can ne be bei tomange wucakke cenin dor mwer bou na cer nen.
La ci an kungum nen dii na mo fwere biwure, tero nin.
La Yeecu yii co, “tokum toke, mani mwa cuwa Teluwe mwe kwama ti”.
La kambo bwekelkele dim cuwa Yeecu keri, concu dubomco biduwar bwiri.
La Yeecu yilaken Galili ki kwan yuwa tangber kwamari. La fulen dor ce reu curongi cinanloro kentangum wiye.
La can yoten merengkako bi kur waber, La gwam caklang co ti.
La con bou Nazaret fiye ci yom co wiyeu la kambo ci lerum maka, con doken mor bi kur waber kakuk folokak, la kwen con titiye na kiye kiye ka ki dir.
Cinne co bifumer Nii Dukume kaya, la con fiye wo mulangi,
Yuna tangber kwamaka wi dor miri wou cin cor meu timuwang dor na ne fulen kerero ken fiye nob bwen wiyeu. con tuom ye nan kwa dir fiye nubo ci tabangtabangeu, kange nee ka tokak fukmatinimbonin na kwin nubo ci neten dotange tiyeu.
Nan kwa dir cor cini kwamar
La con cumom bifumer ne riwo timwiyeu. La con yii ken, nuwe nubo gwam bi kur wabero rime ki tokanco.
La con yoten kan co yii ci keroti duwen bifumer wo dim fo ki nuwaka kumek.
Nubo gwamwi tok kero ken dor cer la citi Nyumangi kange luma kereko ceru ti Nyiceu. La cin me”wo kebo bi bwe Yucufu ka?”
La con yii ci, “Bicom kam yii dangke wo kom ki Nii Twaka Twam dor mwero. Dikewo ma duwa ma ma kafarnam meu, ma dong=dong nyo cinan lormwer.
La con toki Bicom ma yii komti, nii Dukume kange win wo fiyom bo yoka we cinan lor cer.
La mor bilenker ma yii komti, natub kwalebo kila kabo mer Icraila, tiberoco Iliya wiyeu, la biloro mungum na coro ta'areceu kange cuiyakko mukkun, la wura dor bou bitine corin.
La ci tun bo Iliya win ciye nin. La tunco Jerefat cidone, nawiye kwale kange yimwiyeu.
Walebo kala kabo mor Icraila kwama Ilica nii dukumeu, win wo ci twabo, kan Na'aman wo ciria.
Nubo gwam mor bikur wabereu funero tamci kambo cinuwa kero weri.
Cin kweri cin cokken co buiko cinan lore ci ya ken kico kong cueli wo ci mum cinan lor ciro dor cereu na ci tungu co bitine.
La ca ci cum tiber ciyer co yaken kange fiye.
La con yiraken kafarram cinan loro kange mor Galili, la con yoten kange co merang cinenti ki kakuk fobkak.
Cin ma nyumanka ki merankaceko, wori co ki tok kero ki Bikwanked.
La mor bi ker waber nii kange wi wo ki yuwa kelkelike, la con cii ki dira dur.
E' ye nya mam ti ki mo Yeecu Banajara, mo bou na mo twalangum ne? min nyumom mo co nii wucak kwama ce.
Yeecu ca kelkeliyomin tor, yii, tok re ker, ceru mor nii wo. kambo kelkeliyo jwa nii wo mer ken bitine tiber ciyer la ce rum mor nii wo, nuwa cinen bo tura ki kange nure.
Nubo gwam ti nyumangi, citi tokkami buiti ciye lan ker ye na wo? Co yii kelkeliyo kero ki nyial kange bi kwankered lan cerum.
La nyou, cin ter tokka fulen cero cinan loro kantangum wiye gwam.
La Yeecu dubom bikur waber ro doken lo cimonne, la fer cimon kalati ki kwirom bwi, la ci ken keri dor cer.
La kwen con titye dor cer, co ca kwirum bwi min tor, kwirum buiyo dubomco, dandang con kwemim con ta maka yiroko.
Kambo kakuko yar ken tiye ni, rubo bou cinenti kirubo nuwa bo luman tuirako ki dimen ki dimen, con yo ti kang ceko dor ciyer gwam con twam ci.
Kelkelibo cerangu mor nubo kila kila ken. Cii wiyeti ci ti toki, “mo bi bwe kwama,” Yeecu ca kelkelibo ca dob ci bo tok ker, wori cin nyumem con co Kritti.
Kambo fini celumen con cokum dor ce ki kwace fiye nob mani yeu, nubo ducce docoti co lo ci bou fiye co wiye, cin mani na ci kicim na dob cire.
La con yii ci man nee fulen kerer liyar kwamaro tangrim cinan Lorenbo. Won co dike bwi ci tumum ye fe.
La con ter neka fuleneko mor bi kur wabero Yuhudiya gwam.
La yilam kambo nubo mwerum fiye Yeecu wiyeri ci nuwa ker kwamaro, la co tim kang catiyo Janisarat deu.
Con to na bire mwenge yo tirangum wi kong caji nin, nubo ta'a jinge cerangum morece nir biliyar ciyer ti.
Yeecu kwiken mor Nabire mwengek ro win wuro ki cimonreu, la con yii co a kutaka ten ki nabira mwenge bi dob mor mwenge. La con yii ken mor nabire mwengek ronin, la co merang nubo ninti.
Kambo co dim kere di, con yi cimon, kob babire mwenge yaken ciko fiye cuwa cuwau, na mer ken biliyar mwero na taka jinge koce.
Cimon yii co “Teluwe, nyo ma nangen kume del nyo taba kange diker wi. La ki ker mwero mamer ken biyaro mor.
Kambo ci maweri, ci ta jinge ducce la biliyar ciyero ti biyetangi.
Coci ken farub nangeneb ci bo buro nabire mwenge wineu bo na tikanci, cin bou cin dirongum nalire mwengeu ciro yabcite, la cin teri kulkako.
La Bitru kambo to Yeecu ri, yarken bitine duwen yeelur la coki, kubom minen, wori min nii Bwiran ke “Teluwe”,
wori con nyumami, kange nubo buro kange ceu, ki kilaka jinge ko ci tabe.
Wuro mwerum kange Yakubu kange Yuwana bi beyo lo Jabadi farub nangeneb cimaneh. Yeecu yii ciman cuware tai, wori nawo kange kab mwa ta nob.
Kambo ci cokum nabire mor mwengecin yoken konge, cin dubom dikero gwam cin buangcinenten.
Kambo co ki no win mor cinan lonironineu, kange nii wi dim ki tuirak walek, kambo co to Yeecu ri con yar ken ki tikob ceb la conken co, tokti, “Teluwe” Namo ti ci ri mwantuamye cerum”.
La Yeecu ta'ar, kang ce ko keco toki mati cui, yilam wucak, dangjang waleu dubom co.
La con yi nii co a yi kange nii, la yii co, ya mure mwe, na nung dor mwero nii waber nin na ne tii kako ficang ngeu. Wo nir mwe ko ceu kambo muca tokeu, na warkero ce cinen.
La kero dor cereu yaken ten kutan, la nuba kila kilau bou wari cinen na ci nuwa co ti merangi na twam ten ci twirani ciyeu.
La mani co cerum ki kwace co yaken ki kob diloti
Yilam win mor kumeniwo co merangkatiyeu faricawa, kange nob merangka wer funer ci yiirongum wi buri ci bourangu muan loro Galili kange Yahudiya kange Urchalima gwam. Bekwan Teluwero wi kange co na co twam.
La nubo kange tu kilen do kange dor bilirir, la ci to nure wo ci a dokenti co moreu, na cin yoken co bitine kabum Yeecu.
La ci fiyabo nure ci a dor ti ke ceu wori nubo dim kabo, la cin kwiken dor lor la ci cuku co kibi cirico yirau ciko tiber nuber, dong-dong kaa Yeecu.
La co to bilenker ciyereri, Yeecu toki nii luwe, cutan mwen bwiran ker mwero wi.
Nob mulankabo kange faricawa ter meranka keko wo, we wo tok ker Dila karo wo tiye? we a cutan bwiran keti wi kebo kwama win di?
La Yeecu nyam dike ci kwatiyeu, kari yii ci, yebwi ka me wo ti neer kumere?
Co wini bwai be na toke, bwiran ke mweu cutang mwenwi, kwen titi ye yayambo.
La na kom nyumom bi bwe “Nifire” we ki be kwan kere ro for dor bitininer na cutang biriran ker wi, con yii kilendo, man yii nen kwen, tu bicirimeu, na yaken lomo.
Dangjang ko co, co kweri ka bum ciyem la tubiciri ceu wo co dam dor cereu. La cu loco, duktankwama ti.
Nubo gwam wi ti Nyumangi, la ci duktang, kwama cin dim ki tai citi toki, loon to diker nyumankar.
Kambo dike buro ma nyeri, Yeecu cerum kateb con to ni yo der tiyeu dencero Levi yii ku'u yoka duwek, Lacon yii co bwang menten.
Co Levi kwenti bwang cinen ten dubom tangnimdikerenbo gwam
La Levi co cika dur loco, la nob yo ka doreko wi kange tangnim nubembo, kentangum fiye caka carikeu ca carito ti kange ci.
La fariciwa kange nob mulangekab ciyebo wi fuen bibei tomange ceminti toki, ye bwi ko co ko no kange nob yoka duwek kange nob bwirang kere?
Yeecu karci nen, Nubo buro kwamereu mani a do nii Twa ka ti kan co buro nuwa lumau?
Ma buobo na nubo dong dongeu, lan nob bwiran kerek na ci yiloten.
Cin yii co, bibei tomange Yuwana ki, yim, yim Ngak nyo, ki kuom dilo nyo la bi bei tomange faricawa ki manyo ken. La mweu bi bei tomange meu ti cai ti noi.
Yeecu yiici, Nii kange wi wo adok farub bwa yilo na nawite na yii Ngakke, la bwayile na nawiyeu wi kange ci?
La kumeni wi bouti wo ci a tum bwayile ti cineneu, la ki kumeni co ci an yii Ngak.
La Yeecu yiten ci ker Nyuman kar, nii mani a wor fiti kulenti kulen do fuir na curum carko ciko na co ma nyori, can wobrangum kulendo fuir ko, fiti kulene fuir ko mani a datenti carko nin.
La ni kange mani wo a cor ten mwem inabim bo fuir ti mor kole care, naco mani nyo nyori, mwem inabim bo fuir ko an corum koltiye an wuroragum.
La tam a cor inabi fuir mor koltinon fuir.
Nii kange mani wo nuwa kum mwem inabim bofuir tiye, na kweri con nom car kori. La can toki carko la fuir ko
la ma nyo kakuk fobka ko kange, Yeecu yakenti mor to cang ko kange, kange bibei tomange ceu, ci kyang dor canger ti citi kui
la kangem mor faricawa tokiki, ye bwi ka ma dike yorbo ti a mani bi diye kukuk, ka kiye for ka?
Yeecu kar cinen, toti, ka kiye ba dike Dauda mani kwama co co nuwa wuri ti co kange nubo wari kange ceu?
ya mor luwe kwama, con tu cari to tanji laneu ca morece, con nabarubo wari kange ceu ciu cam, bwen no na mam kin nob wabereu ki kwaci cia ca
la con yii ci, bibwe nifire co teluwe kankuk fobka ko
kange bi diye kakuk fobka con doken mor bi kur waber la co meranmbo minti wi, nii kange wi wi wuro kance ko catiyero bwiyam-bwiya
nob mulangkabo kange faricawa to co tibi dor kero can twa nii ni kakuk fobkari na cin fiyan mure wo ci a tamco tiyeu,
la con nyumom dike ci kwa tiyeu la con yii nii wo kangko bwiyame kwen ti fo tiber nubero gwam la nii wo kweni titi wi.
Yeecu me ci yori kebo bi diye kakuk fobka a dike yor yoreu, kaka a ma dike wo yorbeu a cok dume kaka a tual dume?
la con cto ci gwam la co yii nii wo yarken kangmweko, la con manyo, la kang cebo twam
la neer ciyero kayaragum, lacin tok kanti bwiti ciye dike ca ma Yeecu nin tiyeu
lan yilam mor kumeni wo con ceri con yaken bang ca kob dilo con ta kobka dilo kume del co ken kwama ti

denti bi beitomange ceu co buro cimon [wo co caten tak, Bitru ] kange yii Andrawu, Yakubu, Yuwawana, Filibu, Bartalomi,

Yafuja, bi bwe Yakubu, kange Yafuja ckaryoti wo miye co tiyeu,
la Yeecu yirau dor banged kange ci laci tim fiye tuared deu, kange bi bwi tomange ce wila kange nubo kila wo borongu Yafudiya kange wurcalima kange nubo kong caji taya
ci bou na ci buro wo nuwa co na co twam twirani ciyeu, nubo buro nuwa dotange ti ki yuwa kelkelikeu con twam ci ken.
nubo mwerkangum we gwameu dotina ci kem co wori bikwan twa ka ro ceru ti cinen, la con twan ci gwam.
la con to bi bei tomangeceu. con yii ci bibuyer kume kom wo nob bune beu la na kume liyar kwamaro
bi buyero an kume, kom wo konuwa wurati naweu, la ci an bwa kumen fuer bibuyer na kume, kom wo ko ci wiye tina weu, la kan nung nungi
bibuyero na kume to kom la ci ko denkumero na dikero bwir, ki ker bi bwe nir
ko bilangi diye co ko yilam ki for neerer, wori kan fiya cuner dikwama nubo carem cim ma nob du kumebo nin nawo
la kwan nen mo nii mwa cuwe-cuweu, la mom yom mwe dangne mweu
kwan kom nubo wo fuero bwam bwabeu, kan ci wura for kob kwan kom wo ko nung nungi ti na weu, yii kan buwa kan ci wiye ki bui.
kwan kom na nubo tok ti ki wo dong dong di, nubo carem cimbo tok nyo nob dukumeb cwerkebo
la ma yii komti nubo ko nuwa ye tiyeu, cui nii bi dom kange mweu, na ma nubo konene nin dike ro ken
yo nubo cilnen tiye nin bibuyer, na kob nubo buro culong nen ti dor bilenkereu
wo na kwanen ki kang tangal do wineri, neco wineu na kange tum belle mweri tamde mwe
ne nuwa wuro meneneu gwam na kange tum dike kangen na mweri me core moki a bou mwen ciko
kambo mo cuilti nubo a ma mweneri, mo keneu ma ci nen nyo
na moki cuim ka co ka co nubo cuinen tiyeri, in jye yokka fiye mo wiye? bwen na nob bwirang kerer di cui nubo cui ci tiyeu.
na moki mam dikero ken kan co nubo ma mwen dikero ken tiyeri ye yokka fiye weye? bwen no nob bwirang keri ki mam nyo ken
na wo ki ne cen kan nubo mo totiri an yam neneri, ye yokka munen? bwen no nob buiran kerer di ki nem nob bwiram kerero nyou na ci fiya dike ci ne dng-dong
la cui koneneu, na ma cinen dike dong-dong ngeu. ne ken kware kange diker yilau ti, la cuner, kumero na dur, kan yilam bi beyo lo nii dii ko na co con ni lomjome fiye nubo man ki buka kangek kange nubo bwirko
yilam ki cini na wo tee kume nii ciniu
kom mare buolang la mani a ma kumen buolang ti kom kuwa re mani a kuwa komti, tab kangem bo la mweu an tab mwen
kom ne la an ne kom kwele dimdiye, cuwam cuwa, ki bi funger ti con ci an cor kumer ti kan bellik ki kwele ka cuwameu a cuwa kumen ciko
la yila con yii ten ci dangke kange, con toki, fukma an ta fukma nin kangka? na co ma nyon, yaramken buwar gwam citi cimanin nyoka?
bwe tomange labo nii merang ka ceu dur la nubo gwam an yilam na nii merang kako na merang cinendi
ye bwi mo toti ka be yere nuwa kemwe, lamwa tobo cuwemero wo nuwe mweu
mwa yii yimwe myi, moki yii mi tumwen be yere dam mor nuweu, lamoki bwi mwa tobo kukko cuwe mero dam mor nuwe mweu? kom nubo bwir, teri cokum batiye durko nuwe mweu na mo tom yora na mo cokum be yere nuwe yiim weu
la tiyo kendo kange mani wo tu bi tutiyo fuyem fuye tiye, kaka tiyo wo fuyemeu na ne betuti ken
wori tiyo moki nyomco kin bitutico tutiyeu la nubo mani we bituti nying cire ti cuiya ke kaka nubo inabi fiye cilange

ye bwikaco yeti kom ki, teluwe laka bwantenbo dike ma tok tiyeu?
nii wo na bou minen la nuwa ker mereu laco bwang tenen, man yii dii ke co cerkange
co ki no nan nii luwe tiye, woru wobken cuwa mor bitinen la co mu kwar loro ki terenti kwamer lana mwembo dur bouri la came mwegweu kwanan kwar kumeroti laluwe cuwo mani a muka ti wori mum co yora

nyori ma tubo dor miro na nii wo lami mwa bouti cinen, tok ka ker koni, canga mi an kwam.

Luwe kom do wiyeudi, kom ter tok kako kom ki, funeret a no fo luwe wuro.
Tano ni funeret wi luwe nen di, fu neret kumero an yiti luwe nen, no mani dii fowor neret kumero an yila fiya kom.
Kom yi i luwe co, kom ca kom no, dike ci ne kome. Ni nage do daten cor cero, kom dore luwe-luwe.
Bero ci yo komeri kom ca diker ci ti ki kabum kumene.
Kom twam nubo ki bwarakeu wii bitine cuwo, kom yici liyar kwamaro bo bi dom kange kom.
Bitine wo kom do no ci yokom di yaken dor nuret ciyer, kom yi nubo cuwo kom kii ka kwero bitine kume tam na nye ko.
Nyo ferkumen, co warke dor kumer. Be kom nyom liyar kwamaro bo bi dom kange kom.

wuro mani wari kange mo, kiye mati kange mo, take woro mani murti kange mo, watanka co matiye.

Na wo Yunusa yilam yirom nubo nineba, nyo bi bwe nifire a yila yirom ti fiye kalllo wo wiye.

Nii kan mani a kwer talkeri ti na yurangume, kaka Cimon ki tale, dil au yo denkila, be na ne filang mor kuwe.

Kwan kom nob dinglib Farisawa kom yo wine ti dor kwobe na kule, tibi kange tangnim laluwo, dila kom citan wucake kange cwika kwama ko. tam nyo na ma dike dong dong a cwi tangnin dikero tak.
Gwam kume kom nob dinglib Farisawa kom cwiti a nekom fiye ken mor kurwabe, take a ne kom dur yarume fiye fene.

Tak Nii wo koye kabum nobomeri man ko co kabaum nob tomange kwama.
Nii na tok ker kiyer dor bibwe nii fireri an cutan cinenwi. La niwo tok kwilangka dor yuwa tangbeko wucakeri, mani a cutang cinenti.
Tano ci bo ki kom kabom bikur waber di, kange kabum nob bulange kange kabum liyabem kom bwende kange dike ka kartiye nawo ka cerum dor kumerotiye; kange diker ka tok tiye.

We yo yi nii bolange, kange nii do kertiye dor kumer?

Nii wo kwabi neer cer ki, ye ma matiye, wo ma mani ki fiye ma yom carito wo tiye.

La niwo nyombe, la ma dike kebo dong dong, mani a nuwa bi buker kange banjange dutce. Nii wo ci neco dikero ducce a do dikero ducce cinen. Tano ni wo ci neco diker ducce na takako ce, na a do dike ducce kambo ken cinen.

Kaci tociyeri, yici, “yakom dang dor kumero nob waberonin”. Yilam kambo ciyakentiyeri lacin yilam wucak.

Mani atokti, 'iriwo!' Kakaa, 'wurenhim!' Wori Liyar kwaamaro kino tiber kumer”
Yeecu yi nob bwankabo, “Kumeni wi bouti nawo ka yoner toka kume win mor kumeni bi bwe niggire, dilla mani ka toti.
Ciyan yikon, “Tofiren! 'Tofuo!' Dila kom yakomtore, kakaa kom bwangten cire.
Nawo meblankako Nefilanti nafo cunya di kwamaka wori ya ken cunya di kwamako wureno, Nyo bi bwe nii a yilanyo ki kume bokaceko.
Dila kang catin nuwe dotangetinim kidimen kidimen bwiriri, nubo kaleweu ankoco.
Kambo bwi kal Nuhu re, nacuwo tak a bwiuti ki kwama bibwe nii aboutiyeu.
Citi cai, citi noi, citi nai, cinakenti yaken di ye Nuhu doken Nabire kwama la mwom wermakabo bow twalan'gum ci kwarub gwamm.
Nyo cimani ki kwama lutuwe, citi cai, citi noi, citinenii, citi miyei, ci fi fikkoti, cimuran'ngi.
Dila kikakuko Lutu, cerum Saduma, lakira kwaamako caruu dikwama, twalan'ngum ci gwamm.
Nyotak abwiuti ki kume bibweni aboutiye.
Kikakuko wori, niiwo dor kureu ayiraure kica tu kulencer mor luwe. Nyotak niiwo kiyeu ayilaure.
Komkwaki wii Lutu.
Niwo cwidumecetiyeu, anlemco, lano niwo lem dumeceri, anfiyanco.
Miyikomti, kumewo amfiya nubo yob kwangni win. Atim tumwin nadubomwimeu.
Atim fiya natubo yob ci kuwa nerti ware. Atim tum win na dubom win.”

Atim to nubom yob kii, “Antum win nadubom win”.
Yilam netenti dangke kwange ki yori kabo nyirinyir ciya kwo diloti ciya cwaretai,
toki, “Bitine kam'nge nii bolan'nge kam'ngenwi baniki tai kwaama, takri manito yorinubek.
Nawiye kwale kam'nge inwi bitineco, wobou cinenneu, yicoki, 'Tikanaye ka ma manob kiyeb mibonin luma tiyeu.
Inkutan'nyi mani cwiti citikanyco, dila kibwiri toki mor nerece, cano mani cwatan kwaamati, takri mami mito yorak nubekti,
kwarub kan'nge wo nwori nawriye kwalewo kwomye, mantikameo nacifiya luma, kambo marice luwayeti kiboko minenneu.”
Dila Tee kwaama jiki, komuwa dikero nii bolangewo manki tokkeu.
Lanawo kwama mani cor nubolocemboni birombo cicnen wiyeti kume kan'nge kakuke bwini citotika? Anmabwi fiye tikalicika?
Miyikomti, comcorcinen bwimicito wulom. Dilla kambo bibweni bouweri, an kwobti bilam ke nii dor bitinen”
Yilam neten Dankewo kange nubonin birombo ciya ki dorcireu, ki cimnob lumabeb, laci cuwekamten tankne nuboti,
“Nubo kan'ngumbo cin doken mor lo kwama naci kwob dilo-win bwe Faricawa, wineu inni nye dotiye.
Dila bwe Faricawa kweminti, kwodila dor dikero birombo dorcer, kwama, min buwen kang, mikebo natangne nob kwiyeb, nubo mamki cakcakeu, nubo ma burokatiyeu, kakaa namiwo yodotiye.
Mimana kyak kiriti yob mor kume niber. Mine wineuti dorkwobberonin mordike mafiya.
Dila niwa yodiker dorertiyeu tiken kutan, ciyabo nacikun dorcedil, dila kwa cangeang cekoti titokiki, kwaama, ci bruini bwinimito, minni bwiranke.
Miyikombi, niwo yilaken loco fiyam cerke, kebo nawineu, cawo niwo kunderceri ciyatim yirau kico, lano niwo yiran kidor cero takeri ciyatin kumkenci.
Dila nubo bocinenti kibi beyo naci teici, kambo nob bwankacebo to yeuri cin werankci.
Dila yeecu cuoci fiye ciwiyeu, toki, “komdob bi beyo biduwartinimbo abou fiye niwiye, kom ywacire. Liyar kwaama na kalciroce.
Bilinke miyikomti. canowo yobo liyar kwaamaro bwebi duwari, mani cadoti”.
Kan'age dur nubere kan'nge mecoki nii meranka dike yoryore”, ye ma mati nsa fiya dume mankidike?
Yeecu ciyaco, “Yebwi mucoye ni madike yoryoretiye? Nikange mani womadike yoryoretiyo nobons kwaama win cardi.
Mwa nyimom werfudo-mare kayaka, twaldini, kure kwii, cwerde cwerke, ne Tee mwe kan'nge Nee mwe durko”.
Di liyawo yiki, minmamwo kwarub kikwama min bwebwoyileu”.
Kambo Yeecu nuwa nyeri, yico. Dikero win cwar kumwene. Miyem dike mucikeu kwarub, neken nubowe mancikeu, manfiya lo kwaama-ladina bou nwangmenten.”
Kambo nicuwaka nuwa dikero biromberi, kan'ngum nercerobicom, wori cinni cuweka kamboken.
Kambo Yeecu tonercoro kayommeri, lantoki, “An bwai nob cuwakab nidokin liyar kwaamar.
Atim yilam bwarinin naa Telemeko nadoken buwak bilifarak, kan'nge ni cuweka doken liyar kwaamar.”
Nubowa nuwa keroweu nyoki, “nokino nyori we abumtiye?”
Yeecu ciya, nike lambi kwannifireu, deker makar fiye kwaama nuyeu.”
La Bitru intokiki, “Nwo, nyin dubom dike nyicikeu kwarub nyin bwangtennen.”
Yeecu nyici, Biki cwom nikan'nge nani dob locuti, kakaa wice, kaka kebcebo, kakaa Teebcebo kakaa bibiyoloceu, ker liyar kwaamar.
Lamamica fiyati kiriti kiriti fo kalewenin, kan'nge dume diriye kalewo boutiyenin.
Kamboci mwerci kwocilombo yoberi, nyici, “Inno, biyakenti wurcalima, kwarub dikoro ci mulan'ngi dor bi bwe niner kan'nge kang nobtoman'ngeb dukumebeb atim dim.
Ciyar nekanco kan buboko yombo kwaamau, ci buwoco, cineco dofan'nge, citwomcinen bitom.
Ciyam malico, citwalumco, ankwenum ki kume taareu”.
Dilaciyom winwo mor dikerobirombonin, wori kerowo yuran'ngum yuran'nge fiyeciwiyeu, ci yomtenbo dikeci tokeu.
Kambo cidadom Jeriko, ri fukwa kan'nge inwo yimcun'nya nurek, kenkiniti,
kacinuwa kalinube cukentiyeri, lacinme nye bweitiye,
Yeecu Banazret cuken tiye.
Dila fukmau kundir kibikwan tokkero, “Yeecu, bibwe Dauda, Cibwini mito. Dala birombo kabeu werangco, ciyicoki kumwom.
Dila kunten diro kibi kwan kamboken inyiki, “Bibwe Dauda cibwini mito.
La Yeecu tim inyici ciyaboukico cinen. Kambo fukma bou bidomer, La Yeecu meco,
ye mu cwitin mamwene? “inyiki, Tee kwaama, micwitin tofiye.”
“Yeecu inyico, “yotoka fiyeko, bilinkemweu nirumnen.”
Wi dangjang fiya toka, kwangteng Yeecu, duktang kwaamati. Cito nyori, lanubo kwarub caklang kwaama.
Yeecu do yarico la cukenti morece.
Nikange wi deu cero zakka, dur nobo yo dortiye, nii cwika,
Con mani no co to keno we yecudi. La co dol bo toka wor, nobo durce, take con nii bi kwen.
Laco cukken kab ya con kwiken tii nyincin naco tom co, wori Yeecu acuwi fonure cuwonin.
Kambo Yeecu lau weyeri kung nuwe dii layico ki zakka yi rau wulom daten mwo da lomo.
La yilau wulumm-wulum yuwo co ki fuwor neret.
La gwam ciye cin to wori, ci ma fwennati ki, ya fura lo nii bwiranke.
Zakka kweni tii, ki to Teluwe, man. Kabkangum cweka miko more yob nane fuwa wine tana man yodiger nii cum wo ma yotiyeri, ma yila neti kiriti na'ar.
Yeecu yi coki duwen fuloka bou fo luwe wurini nii co bi bwe Ibrayim.
Bi bwe nii bo na do kange fuloka nobo leme.
Di di nuwe digewo digewo nyer. Con yoten coti tokki ki danke, wori co bi dom kange Urcalima. Cin tuken liyar kwamaro biyeken nawo.
La con yiciki nii dur cu bitine kange, ya ca yo liyar na co yilam.
Con co, cangace kwob, la yi ciki kom yila kangi, ko tiye kom miye nakom fiya mwen dorcet, mimale yilau.
La nobo loce ko co, cin twom nob bwiko cek ki manya ciya ti niwo a ca ciyar dor nyer.
La ci ne nii wo liyoro, kambo co bou lo weri co tomi ki ciya cucine ne congetini na co nyomom kiyemero co ne ciyeu ki ciya yila kalakangtiyeu.
Wi kabako be cinen ki Teluwe fam mwem bo we ma fiya mwen dorcet, fambo kwob.
Liya yi co ki dong dong canga ken, wuri mo, maken dor dike bi dure, man nenen tako cunnucut do kwob.
Na yobe ce bo yitiki fam mwembo Teluwe ma fiya mwembo fam bo nung.
Liya yicoki tom cunnukirning mwo tamciko.
Na taarece bo yitiki, fam mwembo wo man yo ken co yora mor kulene,
man nuwa tai mwe to, wori mor ni funere, moki to tike mo yobe, mo biye dige mo fii be.
Liya yi co ki ki ker mwer ma mamwer bo langtiye, mwo cange bwit mo nyomon moki mo man nii maki to re dike ma yobe,
ye bwi mo yobo ki kye miro fiye bini kiyeme no bwiko ma bori na yo co ki mwen.
Liya yi nobo tin wiye, kom yom fam bo co tan cike, kom niken niwo ki fam bo kwobbe.
Ciki Teluwe, wii ki fam bo kwob.
Miki niwo ki dikereri, cin yok cinen ten, niwo man cikeri an yom tangnin bo cine nen.
Ki nobo biro koki yilare liya ciye kom bo ki ci fiyemi wii na twallangum ci fo kami.
La kambo co to kan nyeri cui ken Urcelima.
Kambo cibo bidom kange Betafaji kange Betani dor bange ci coti ki zaitun, co tom nob bwangka coko nyo yob.
Yi ciki, kom ya cuinukur do wureno ka kome. No com yari kanto be gelba kange tekum we kom kwiu. Kom bou men ciko.
No nii kange me kom ki, 'Ye bwiyi kom kwi tiyeri? kom yi co ki teruwe cuitiye.
Nobo biro cu tom ciyeu yaci, fiya be gelba na wo Yeecu yiciyeu.
Kambo ci kwi be gelba tiyeri, nob gelba me ciki, ye bwi ci kwi gelba tiye?
Ciki teluwe cuii tiye.
Ci bo Yeecu nin ciko, cin miti kuleu ciye ro dor be gelba, co ci kun Yeecu ci yoti dorcere.
Kambo yaken tiyeri cimiten kulen ciyero ti dor nure
Di con dedom yirakako kong zaitun, la nob tomange ceu cin ter bilantumbo ci wab kwamati ki diro dur wori nangeu nyo mamka ci to we.
Bibwiyer lamiyo fiye liya wiyewo boti den Tere fuwor neret firen dii kwama kange yorkako wo na duk kakoce.
Kangum Fariciyawa mor nob mwe kanka nyico ki ni murangka kwanan nob bwingka mweko.
Yeecu yilci miyikum bi rin keti bwenteno nobo biro kumom di terentiyo ki bwiyici ciya bi lange
Fiya Yeecu bou bidomri la ci lam bero cori la com ciwiyeu dor cer
tok ki, waki kom nyomom dike abou ti ki furnare di dila cumom nuwi kime mani ka to ti.
Dila diye boli mwinen, wo nob ki Yeecu mwe, ciyan mu ki yalange kentangum nen, ciyan kwenang mwenten culang ko gwam.
Ciyan kun kom bitine wari kange bi beiyo lomwe. Mani ciya dob kange terti dor kecer wori mo kabo bati fiya kwama cwinco tiken nenen.
Yeecu do bicor wabe co la tir yuwanob miyankake,
yi ci ti ki mulangum mulange lomi a yila lo diko, kom yilam bwak nob kwiyeb.
Yeecu wi merang kang kang mor bikur waber. Dila dur wabero kange nob mulanka kange nobo dor noberoci cwiti na ci twallumco.
Di la ci fiya bo nor maka, wori nobo cuwati ti cinen kambo ken.
Kange diye Yeecu merangti mor bi kurwabe, la tok furen kereuti nubo wabereu kange nubo dur ko.
Ci tokeroti ciye coti yiyo kibi kwan kero wini mon mam nan do wotiye. We nenen bi gwamdo woo.
La co ciya ciki meki kero mangmekom tiye nyo.
kange yuka mwen Yohana yerau di kaka nii fire nenka?
Cin kobkanti, bwetici ciki tonou biki di kwamari anyiki yebwe bo nebo birinke cinenen.
Na la duwareu bi yi biki nifiro nendi no bo gwam cinye mobangbe ki ter, wori cin ciya mor mereciye Yohana nii to mange
Cin ciya ciki yombo keno ki no feri.
Yeecu yi ciki moken nyo mani yikamti keno kibo gwando wini ma man dike biromtiye.
Yi dubo danke wo kange nii yunkake inabi co ne kange nom tonen toka takeko conyaken bi ti ne kange ya daranyi kutangnyi.
Ki cwakiya bika bituweka ram cuii tom kange ceka ce ayo nob tone bone, beri naci neco mor dikero teige neneu. Di nob tonebo ci bunk, ci yoco kang koni.
Tom cenge ce tak ci bungco, cine co dotange, ci yweco kan koni.
Tomtange na ta'ar ce cin nuwacine der, cin merkeco kare.
La nii take Inabi ki, nye ina matiye? ma tom bi bweni macui.
Dila nob tone bo toco citokange bwitici, wo co nii coka gwarito bo twallum na kwalito yilam be.
Ci mwobken co bwiyim taken cin twallum co. Nyen teeluwen taken Inabi amaciticuke.
An bou na twallungum nob take bo wo na yila na neke nubo kenge takeu. Kambo ci nuwanyeri ciki, kwama acukum.
La Yeecu toci layiki.
Nii wo yar ti dor terero wonineri, an wurorangum. No nii wo tero yelti dorowonineri anfwoyok tamgum co.
Ci nob murangkako kange nobo dur waber cin cui naci tomco nawo wori an nyomom ki tokerewo dor ci, la ci cut an rubero.
Ci derangecoti cin tom nobo atoutiyeu wor ranyonri nubo weceke, na cifiya lentanke mor lekamor kercono ni, naci nekenco borank kange bi gwam nii dure.
Ci meco, ki Nii merangkan nyo yumom muki toka kange meranka dike donge donge tekeu kange nii men nawo dong bwinge kerdiye, muki merangka birin ket dor nure kwama.
Mino werfune ka no ya kemer dor kaicar, nin kaka o ong?
Yeecu nyomom yulkar yici.
Nugmen dinari wuro wee, takeu munranka we dor cereu? ciki, “ki kaicer dike na kaiceroce komne kwama dike na kwace?”
Nob murangka kange dur tini nob wabe bere cifiya bo diker bitore mur keu ceroni.
nubem. Cin nyemruki ki cuka kan cone, ci tobo kangeker.
Kam cadukiyawa cibo ficowege, nobo wo yitiki gwamka tuke mani.
Cin meco ciki “nii merangka” Musa mulang nye nen ki, no ni yiki no yini bwi yamdi, nii ki nawe la manki bibwe, nyice anan nawiye, afiya nyicenin bwe.

Inyo wo yobeu.
