Tabti anwo yaken ciko ka-nge a kwomyere, wori mi tumki yirom Yesum bwimi.
Luma Teluwebe Yesu abwangten ka-nge yuwatangbe kume ko, kebmibo. Ati nyo.
Bulus ni tomange Yeecu Kiriti ki ci yaka fiye kwama, kii nubo coccoke na kwama yim Afisawa borom bo ma bilenketi mor Yeecu.
Naweu luma kwama ko ati kange kom kange fuwor nener fiye kwama Tee be kange Tee kwama Yeecu Kiriti.
Caklanka ki Tee kwama Yeecu Kiriti co ci nebo bibwiyere ki bibwiyer tinimbo wuyakiwo mor nenero lumako ceu mor dii kwama mor Kritti.
Nan yi me felka kaleko mor Yeecu. co kombo nabi yi yimbo wucakke kange yambo maniki duti kaceu.
Mor cwika kwama dangi ki naci tumbo nabi yilam bibwece fiye Yeecu Kirirti wiyeu. Ci ma wo kambo ci cwiti naci mane.
Cune inco kwama naci yo caklanka wo duktangka luma nererk ko ceu. won co dike nebo kang nyam aya fiya bwe nerece wiye.
La mor bwe nere ci ceerbi fiye bwiyale ce kange tabka bwiran kerer fiye luma nererce ko lalame.
Cin ne luma nererkowo, Lama nyo mor nyomka gwam.
Kwama yibo bilenke dikero wuro yurangum yurangeu. Ki nyomka ce kange dikero gwam dii kwama kange dor bintiner mor Yeecu.
Cin cokbo almasihu nabi yilam nob kwaleb na kwama ce.
Mor Kritti cin ma binen ywelka ko wo kika mor ywelka cek, cin ni ma dikeroti gwam nawo nerceroceu.
Kwama man yo wori nabi fulom na caklanka duktanka ceko cekoceu. inbo nob kababo bifiya yoka neroko weu mor almacihu.
Mor Almacihu kom fiya nuwaka kerbileng kerer, ker dumer ber fiya Yeecu wiye. morece kom nebilenker ci dokkume kang ki Yuwatanbe kwama ko wucakke woci ma kumen mor cereu.
Yuwatanbe ko inco ciyaka kwali beko na nyime yabi fiya. wuro na caklanka duktanka cek.
Naweu, ki kwama mi nuwau fulen bilenkerer kumero mor Ubangiji Yeecu kange cwikacek yaken ciko kwarub birombo cii cokci kercereu.
Ma kurong bo kwaka ki kom mi kwob kimen diloti mor dilotinim.
min kwob kumen dilo miki Tee bwe wo di kwama Yeecu Almasihu Tee wo wucake ane kom yuwa tangba ceko wo ba fiya bukati cikeu kange wo nyomka cek kwarub.
Mi kwob diloti na nuwe kume wumom nakom nyimom ciya bicore kumeko. Mikwob diloti nakom nyimom cuweka liyar kwaliero mor birombo ci cokunnaceu.
Mi kwob diloti kom yimom liyard cero wuro na dur wuro mankidi more benen wuri bine bilenker dwikako wuro kino fiye nanyer kwaner bikwan nerer cet.
Wonka bikwan durero ci mam nagen ciko mor Almasihu ki kwama wo kwama kunco tuweu yokenco kanko cacciyere mor di kwama.
Cin yo kenco dor birbishi kange Liyar, do ka, lo dako wannen irin liyar can yoken Almasihu kebo na kele wuro ce ki kwaco dila kange kalewo bouti yeu.
Kwama dokken dikero gwam mor Bibwe kwama cin yonco dur dor dikero nen gwam mor nub bwanka ceko.
Nub bwanka ko in bwico, dika niwo dim dikero gwam mor dikero gwam, gwameu.
Dila nan duwo kom bwambwa mor bwirang ker kumer kange kanke.
More ce kom yim yim kumem bo wo dor bitinerowo kom bwanten niwo ma yila bikwan tini diyok kwamak, won co yuwako ma nagenti, mor bibei bi kwan doret.
Nanduwo gwambe bi mor nubo birombo nebo bilenkere bibwang ten ka dikero bwirko bwibe cwitiyeu. bi matika nagen bwiyer kange dike nerbero katiyeu. fo bwiri bibei wuro daten funer kwamareu, na kangem.
Dila kwama nii ci bwini tenagi nye, ni ker wikaro ci cwibo manki dika.
Kambo bibwiyam bwiya mo bwirangke, bouki bo mor nero funer wari kange almasihu. ci fulobo kin luma nerer cek.
Kwama kunbo wari dila yobo biyi ari nawo, win mor Almasihu Yeecu.
Ci ma wuri ker kaldo wuro bouti yeu. na daang cuyeka luma nerer cko fiye Yeecu wiyeu. Kdang binen wuro kino luma neret cek.
Naweu ci ceerbo kin lumanerek wo bilenkeroceu wo kebo fiye kom wiye, luma nerek kwamak.
Kebo dor nagenent nawori kange kume a kunde dor.
Bin nagen kange kwamar, fwelfwele mor almasihu Yeecu nabima nagen do ken, birombo nanduwo kwama yowau nabi, yi yimbo moreceu.
Naweu kom kwabi nanduwo kom nubo yombo kwama ki yim bwiyeme. ci ki cuwoki “nubo biyebo Lave” dike ci coki biye Lave bwiyeu wuri kan nube ko matiyeu.
Dila ki kwama wo nacin kab kangum kuke da almasihu. kom fabub nubo Israila nin. ko fabub ker neret. Kom manki yomka dor finir. Kom manki kwama dor bitiner.
Di la na weu mor almasihu Yeecu kom wo nanduwo kutan kange kwama, cin bou ki kom bidom fiye buyale almasihu.
Cin co fuwor nener bero. La naci yilam win kiyobeu. Mor bwiyece cin bubam tiyak kiyeko wo kab kangum bo kange bwitibou.
La naci tungum warka kowo ki nyaleu kange werfuneu, dila naci fwel nii fwir win more ce. makako nyeu bou ki lumanerek.
Ci manyo naci mwer nubo yob mor bwiye wi kange kwama fiye yeikaka. Fiye kwoblom bwatiyeu cin twalum kiye tiber cereu
Yeecu bou makimen ker fuwor nener kom wo km kutan kange kom wo kom bidomeu.
Na fiye Yeecu wiyeu kwarubbe yobeu win mor yuwa tangbak cek biki nure yakenti Tee nenneu.
Naweu kom nubo yombo kwama wni wo, kebo fabub. nawori faub ari knage birombo cokcokeu wo kwama cer farub, nangeneb.
Birombo ci mu ci dor kwar nob tomangeb kange nob ker dukumeb. Almasihu Yeecu ki dorcer coci lanrang Tee mukare.
Mukako mwer morece kwarub, ci diti na lo kwama mor Ubangiji.
Morece ci mu kom tiye gwam kom yilam fiti yim kwama mor yuwa tangbecek.
Lana wori, mo Bulus bwe furcina ker almasihu ma kom nubo yombo kwama.
Mi kwati kom nuwam don nager do dur ko wo luma kwama ceu neken mor ker kumer.
Mi mulankumen dor dukumero ci yi yereu. won co bilnker yurangum yurangeu ma tokker dor cer mor bifumero kange.
Kambo ko fiye dor cereu, kan nyimom basira miu mor yuranka bilenker don amlsihu.
Wuro kaltiyo nanduwo i yi cibo nubo. la na weu cin dang nob tomangeb bo nen kange nob tomangeb dukumeb. cokum coke mor Yuwa tanbe.
Kero wo yurangum yurangeu, in co ker kwarowo dangi nubo nyombo kwama faub kwalib wari kange bo, kutelti mor bwiye win. Farub mwerkankab wari mor nortimin almasihu Yeecu fiye kerkwamari wiyeu.
Wonco dike bwi mi yilam canga fiye yomka luma kwama nekye nawo durbi kwaner cero.
Kwama neyi nyomka kowe. canno min coni dual duwale mor birombo cokeu na kwamace, nan tok ker kwama nubo nyom bo kwama nin don cuweko almasihu wuro manki dika.
Nan fetang nubomin gwam dike kwama ywelcinentiye bilenkero wuro yurangum yurangeu wo coti coti kwama yurangumeu, co cinnir fweldiko gwam.
Nawori fiye ku wabero nob bidweb kang nubo ma liyar diko kwama tiyeu, ciyan nyimom yomka kwama fiyeco ki dimen kidimen.
Wuro bwi nyo nawo co ci mani mor Almasihu Yecu Tee be kwama.
La mor bibwe kwama bin wiki bikwan nener ducce, kange ciyaka kiker bilenkerbe morece.
Naweu mi kenkomti kom cwaretai kiker dotange mi nuwa kerkumereu wo yilam duktang kumen keu.
Naweu min cunti ki duwenmir kabum Tee.
Wuro fiye ciwuye ci cuwanga nuboti wuro kwama kange bitineu.
Mi kwobdilo cin ciya kumn dor cuweka duktankace. kom biner kambo ken ki dur bikwanererowo yuwa tangbanko mineu wo more kumeu.
Min kwob diloti Almasihu ayi mor nener kume ki bilenker ke mi ker abdilo ti tak kom tim yora kom mum yora kambo kem mor cwika cek.
Kom yilam mor cwika cek wori na nyimom, kange nob bwanka kwama wari wuyak, in ye cuwaka, kange kuyaka, kange cuwemka cwiki almasihu.
Mi kwobdiloti na kom nyimom tenanka cwika almasihu wo cum nyonka. Kom mawo naci dimkom ki dika kwamak.
Naweu wo ki dur bi kwaner maka dikero bi kenu kaka kwanka nerer bisaga dur bi kwaner cer manangenti more beu.
duktangk a yilam nace mor fiye wabka fiye Yeecu wiyeu yaken ciko ki curom tinin diri diri Atinyo.
Nawo ri nawo min mi furcineu ker kwama mi kenkomti kom yi yimbo daten kange bi co kwama makemeneu.
Kom yilam ki dikero ken do wu a mati ki dikero ken kange birom nenerem. Kom yo kebkume bo mor cwika.
Kom yi yim mwerka dorek mor yuwa tangbek kom morum mor fuwor neret.
Bwiyo wi win kange yuwa tangbekko win, kam ci co kom dor yoka nerer ko wineu.
Kwama win bilenke win, kange yuka munge kwama win.
Kwama win kange Tee gwam. Co ci dor diker wuyake, fiye wuyake, kange mor wuyak.
Kwama ci nebo nyomka dong dong kange cuwaka nyka almasihu.
Nawo cin bwanten kange cannya mo dotange cin ma nubo ki yomka.
In ye tok tiye, “Cin kwiken” kiyi yiram, yaken bitine more cuwa cuwau.
Co ci yiraweu co ci kwiken dikwama ci mawu naci dim dikero gwam.
Yeecu Nii ne nub yomka nawuro nyo nob tomangeb, dukume nubo waker cero fiye nubo to kwamatiyeu, kange nob merangkatiyeu.
Cima nyo na ywellum nob kwama bo na maka nange neke ce, na mum bwi almaihu.
Ci manyo nabi lam yim bilnker bo ken bo kange nyoka bibwe kwama. ci manyo la bi lam dwika, na birombo lam dim dur cero lo Yeecu.
Yecu muu wuro nyo kati yelo bi yilam na bi bei. ka cita yilang boti. Wuro nyo kati yoli bi yuwa merangka binen kankak kange buyelangka nob maka cwerkeko.
Nyori ban tok bilenker mor cwika wori nabi dwi mor bi kwanner cer, co cin durken mor Yeecu.
Yeecu mwerum bwi nob neka bilenker. Bwiyo mwerum mwere fiye kulteltinim bo wiyeu, na bwiyo duyom na mum dencero mor cwika.
Naweu nii makumen be wereti mor kwama miki kom cwobtende yimbo na yim nubo nyombo kwama cimati yim azanci bang da wofi wo manki nageneu.
Cin fim kumti cile mor kwaka nerer ciko fabub ki dume nawo kwama ceu, fiyu bwin nyo ka cek wo more ceu kange wo kwamka nerer cekeu.
Ma ci nuwa kwenduwe ti cin neken dor ciro nagen mor bwiyer maka nangendo yeyeu kange la cin merang kenti ki dikero bwir.
La kebo nyo kom merang nage kwama re.
Min kwatiri kom kweri, kom nuwam dorcer. mikwatiri cin merang kumen morece, nawo bilenker Yeecu nyeu.
Yii nen ki tam dikero nanduwo mwa merangeu, kom yii yimkumenbo nanduwo, la nii cer nii carko yakcanti ki bwirankeret ceko.
Kom minang nii carkowo naci mirim kom fwice mor yuwa tangbe kumek.
Kom manyo nakom dum ni fwir wo cerkan kwama ci fwel mor bilenker nere, kange wucak kange bilenke.
Na wori kom cutan cwekewi, “Tok bilenke kange nii bidom kange mweu,” wori bin kuteltin bwitibo.
“Kom kanngum ner, dila mare bwiranke”. kom dob re ka kuko ayarum kom kang nerek.
Kom nere bwe kelkele nyilo.
Ni ku kumtiyeri adubom kuka kuyeko tak. La nyi co liya mananngen manangen ki kanice naci fiya dike catikan nubo kwambe ti cikeu.
Kero fwemfweu acirangum nyi kom. No nyori, kom ywelten dor kumero na ne luma nubo nuwatiye.
Kom kande yuwatangbe kwamako nin ner fo fiye ciweu ci dok kumen kange nawo kaku ceer kako ceu.
Kom cutan fur nerero win, da hasala. fush da tankiya da reny da dukan mugunta. kom ma bwiti kume nen dikiero ken, kom yilam ki nero yiber.
Kom dob keb kume bo bwirangker cero kambo kwama kume Yeecu dob kumen bwirang ker kumeru.
Nuweu Kom ma meranka ki kwama na be beyo cwitiye.
Kom yi yimbo mor cwika nawo Yeecu cwibeu latak neken dor cero dike luma neret kange diker ne kar fiye kwama wiyeu dorber, twika dikero fican fican diker yokar fiye kwama wiyeu.
Burotum kange kwarub kayaltum, kange kaya kaya kawowo yei nyeu ciya cuwo kome more ce, nyo daten kinob bwangka kwama.
ciya cuwo re batsa ker kulerner kange alfasa birombo daten bem. No nyori biyilam nob buka kangek.
Naweu kom nyi mom ni kayaka kange ni mani wucakeu.
Kangem abolkome kiketito bwir. in co dikero birom bo funer kwamaro boutiye dor bibeyo bonya nyi nyeu.
Kom mwerkan re dor wari kange ci.
Wori naduwo kom kunta cile dila naweu kom filan mo kwama. Dila kom yayambo nabibei filange.
Wori nange filange ro co lumako, luma nerek kange bilenke.
Kom do dike kwama ma funner nerer ti cikeu.
yorekan nange do wo manki yorako ken kange nagen do kumtacile dila yora a womci.
Diker kwenduwe kange duka diker ci mani yurangum yurangeu.
Diker gwam cano filang danciri ciki tom nyo.
Wori diker yilam ci to ti filange ri co diker bwi citoki wuram mo ni dume kwenum mor buware, Yeecu atim ne filang dor mwer.
La na weu kom mayora mor timbo kom tim kumentiye.
Kom tiyora kange maka nangenek ki kanka neret wori kume cwiku n bwi.
Na wori kom yakcare ki nyom wori kang yim nimti lanyori kom dim ki yuwa tangbe kwama wucakkeu.
Nyori kom nore dikero bwir wo a yokom ti mor dotangeu, daten di kom dim ki yuwatangbe kwama,
Kom ki tokkan kero ti bwiti kume kon ki zabura kange nuwe kange nuwetinim mor nerer kom, kanuwe cakkeu ki ner kumer fiye kwama wiyeu.
bak ni bak kom ne bilenker keti wori dikero gwam mor den Yeecu Tee be kwama.
Kom Ciya kom tum dotange bwiki kume mor neka kwama
Natub kom bwanten dir nabarub kumebo mun kom ki man ki kwama.
Wori bwayile co dur wicero nawo almasihu dur nub bwanka kwamak co ni fuloka bwiyeko.
Dila kambo nub bwanka kwama ko neken durcero tiye, tamyo natubo ciya bwece dur gwam.
Nabarub kom cwit natub kumebo kambo Yecu cwi nub bwanka cekeu. ya neken dor kercer.
Ci ma nawo na ciyim ci wucak. Naci nirimbo ki mwom nikam fiye kercero wiyeu.
Ci ma oyo naci neken dor cero nub bwanka kwama ko nen wo yoryoreu manki dike kece kulande mani na birombo na wuro dila ca yilam wucak mani ki dwiti.
Na woro nabarubo kom ci natub kumeb bo na bwikom wuro cwi wiceri cwi dorcer.
Ni mani wo kom bwice wiye. Dila neci raritoti cwiti na wo kwama cwiti nub bwanka cebo matiyeu.
Wori bin kutteli kebbeb.
Nyori ni nabare a dubom Tee ce dubo nece citab wice nin ci yob cin yilam nange win.
Dike wo yurangum yurangeu tenanin dila miki tok kange nub bwanka kwama.
Kange o wuya kom nabarobo mon cwi tatumubo nador kumer nawiye kang can can ne bwece durko.

Nyo Tebbo kom kwomde bibeyo lokume a lamde kanka nerer, dila kom mweci mor mwerum mem kwama kange kwobka tuwek.
Kom cangab bo kom bwanten dir Tee luwer kumero wo dor bitinero ceu knage neka durek kange tai kiner bilenker. ma cinen na dimu ki mam ki Tee mwe wo dii kwama.
Kom neci durko nobo wori cito kom tiyeu na kom neci fuwor nerer Nyori kom macinen muni kom ki mam ki kwama kom a ker kwama ro mor nere.
Kom ma dikero kiner kumero wuyak. muni komti bwnate kwama kebo niffir.
Kom nyo diker nimane can fiya yokacek fiya kwama cin nannga ka kaka ci keba.
Kom Teeb Luwe bo kom ma cannga kume nen nyo kom necire dotange kom nyi mom co niwo cin Tee ciu kange kom win kino kwama kom nyi manici dong nyimanka.
Diker wuyak, kom ne bi kwan nerer mor kwama kange mor dur bi kwaner cer.
Kom tu kulen kwener kwamaro gwam na fiya na kom ca kaba dor yulan bwe kelkeler.
Wori kwenbero kebo na nangi ce kange buyale. Dila kange bikwan liyarero wo no warkabo dor bitinereu. wori kaldo kumta cile kange nob kweneb cibo fo mor kalewoninen.
Nyori kom tukulen kwener kwama gwam na ko do lum kom tim kibi kwan mor kwener wonen.
Naweu, kom tim kibi kwan kom bwam dak kumeko mor bilenker kom merumom sulke cak-cakeu.
Kom wuro kambo kom bwam nani kume nakom yaken ki ker kwama lumakoceu.
Mor dikero gwam kom tu kusanko bilenke ko, wuro katwalum bok tinim nii bwir ko cikeu.
Kom tu wambile ker dumero kange kulen yuwa tanbako, wuro ker kwamareu.
Wari kange dilo tinim kange kini kom kwob dilo ngir mor yuwatangbeko kin co nero wo kom kicom wuruti ki birim nerem kange kini ker nub kwama gwam.
Kom kwob dilona yitomange kambo min wumom yimeu. Kom kwob men dilo nan fiyam bi kwan nerer tok ka bilelnke yurangum yurangeu.
Dila na kom nyimom nyim minbo kange kambo mi yimmeu,
Tikikus, kemi macwiti cwiyeu, kange ciyaka cannga mor kwama anyikom co dike wiyeu.
Wonco dike bwi mi two mu co kumen ne wori nakom nyi mom dike nyi more ceu, na kom fiyam yobka nerer mor nerer kume.
Na weu fuwor nener kwama ati kange kom keb mibo ki bilenker wuro Tee kwama kange kwama Yeecu Kritti.
Luma kwama ati kange kom birombo cwi Tee kwama Yeecu Kritti wari kange cwika ko mani ki bwiyaka.
Bulus ka-nge Timoti cangab kiristi Yeesu yã ciko nob kwamab wucake wo Fillibi ka-nge nubo tam ki nubo bwanten kwama tiye, ka-nge nubo durku lo wabbeu. ka-nge nobo durko ku wabbe.
luma kimen ka-nge fuwor neret tebe kwama nin ka-nge Teluwe Yeesu kiristi.
mi bu kwama nin ka-ngeti diye no ma kwa kom ki nere di.
kir-kir mor dilo minin kimen gwam, mi kwob dilo miti ki nero fuwor.
mi bu ka-ngeti dor nangenero bi mati wari mor fulen kere ka cikko ba teruwe ya ciko na wo.
miki bi kwamer neret wo ter nangen ken kimeneu an yaken ciko cwobka di kakuk Yeesu kiristi.
won digero ken nuwa nyo nure wuro dor kimer gwan, nyori miki kom gwam ner mir. kom yilam far nangene mi mor luma, ki bwaka miko ka-nge cerka dorek mik ka-nge tika ki bi kwan bifumero nin.
kwama warke mi, kuru kime gwam mi ciko mor cwika dur wo Yeesu kiristi ce.
wo co dilo mi, cwika kime ko a yokten kab mor merangka ka-nge, ka-nge nyomko diger gwam.
nyori na ko ciye ki dige yor yore gwam na kom yilam nobo ki bilengke, digero bwir mani kimen ya cika dige kiristi.
dim ki bi tutti wucake wo bouti fiye Yeesu kiristi na duktangka ka-nge caklangka kwama.
mi cwi komti ki nyimi keb mibo, dige fiya yereu matikali fiye yokka fulen keret kwama.
bwaka miko mor kiristi bou ki filang nubo lo liya, nubo tõ nub tiyeu gwam, ka-nge kangum bo fiye ka-nge.
kangum yitub beb, ki kinin yilam ki bi kwan neret mor Teluwebe ker bwaka miko, ciki nero kwamer ciya miko keroti man ki taiye.
kangum bo tok ker kiristi ki kor neret ki kwilki-kwilkiye. kangum bo ki nero ken.
nubo ki biye wo ki ma ki cwika, ki nyomka ci bwayere na yilam kucang fulen keret.
nubo wo bwiye ki tok ker kiristi do mor cwika neret ciye, kebo dor bilen keret. ci kwatiri ciyan neye dotange ki fiya cuwo mi bwambwabe.
“la ye” diger win, mor digero gwam, bwen tano ciki ma ki cwerke kaka bilengke. cin tok fulen kwamaro, nyeu, min nuwa luma, ong min nuwa luma.
min nyimom wo a dok cerkamik mor dilo kime ka-nge tikali yuwa kwaman tangbe wo Yeesu kiristi.
miki kuru kang yo neri mani ma nuwa kwenduwe ti, ka-nge ti ka kibi kwang, can ka-nge kicatecc, kiristi an fiya dur kwimi, bwar kaka'a mor dume.
minen “mu ki dumeri, kiristi, no bwar di yokka.
mor bwiyeri, mi nintang wo ti gwam.
la yilam digero bwaibwaye tiber digero wo yobeu. cwika miko na kũbo na ya'a yi ka-nge Yeesu, wo dige yore gwam,
nyeu yilam ki dume, tam nyo ker kimer.
wo min ciya ciko, min nyimom man yim nan bwanten ka-nge kom gwam dor caka kaba ka-nge bilantum mor bilengke.
nyori fiye mi wiye na kom fiya yokka mor kiristi Yeesu no bou kimen takri.
ki ma digero daten fulen keret kiristi, na nyori. no bou mato komri kaka'a mi mani ri, nuwa kimen kom tim kibi kwamer mor yuwa tangbe wucake wiin ki nero wiin, kwilki-kwilki ker fulen keret kwama.
ki nuware tai nubo wuro yilam nob kiye kime. wuro yirom cinen na wuroka ciko ce, kime fuloka kime ko-wuro kwama nin ne.
cin nekom yiber ker kiristi, kebo ka neka bilengke cinen ka-nge nuwa ka dotangen ker cer,
na dontang wo ka to mine neu, la can ka tuwe.
no nekangka bi kwannek wiri no birum neri wiri wi wo cwika netiyeri, no mwer ka-ngka duwe mor yuwa tangbe wucake wiri, no cire duwe ka-nge bunangka wiri,
ko dok bilantum mini bo a dim, nawo ka yilam nero wiine, kom kicwika wiin, ko mwerka-ngum mor yuwako wucake kom ki dige ka yõ kabawiin.
kom mare diger ki cwika duwe kaka'a diger bi boler, nyori ki taka duwe, tu tang ne nube cin lã nen.
kom tore ka dike kom cwitiye koni, nyori kom to dige kangumbo cwitiyeu.
ki nyimom wori ki bwikimi, buro mor kiristi Yeesu.
wori yi yim na kwama dila tũbo dor cerowiin na kwama.

na curo nyori, nyon dubom bi dwir nyero tiber kumer na wuro nee ki mare bi beiyo locenin dangne wi nyo.
no nyori nyi wi ki cwika tiber kumer, kebo ker Almachiya ki kwaco nyo ma kumen tiye dila ka-nge ner nyero ki dor kimer, dige bwiyeu ki cwika nyinen.
kom kwa, kebmibo, ki nangen nyero ka-nge dotange nyeu. kakuk ka-nge kume nyo ma nangenti kati yilo nyi cub ka-ngen kumem mendo nin nangen. ki kwama wuro nyi makimen ker kwama tiye.
kom nob warkeb, la nyo wo kwama ce, kambo nyo yii-yim luma ka-nge liyer ka-nge. ka-nge ker digero bwir wi kumen wuro kom ne bilengke.
no nyori kom nyimom kambo nyo mati ka-nge kom me, kambo tee ka-nge bwe, kambo na wuro nyo nyi kom kere datenne ka-nge wuro fwetang kome nyon nyitin kom dige datenne.
na kom ya yambo daten ka-nge kwama, wuro cuwo kom mwor liyarcer ka-nge duktangka ceko.
co diye bwi nyi bwi kwama nin ti kangka. dige bwiye ki kwama kom yo ker kwamare wi nubo buro ka-nge nubo buro kom nuwa, na wuro yeu ker kwama, wo co kero wuro mannangti kumene wuro kom ne bilengke

kom nuwa yitum mibo, nyon malang kimen kwama bidob, na bilengke ce, kebo mwor nere, nyin ma dige datene na wuro nya to tikob kumebo tiye.

wori ka-ngembo wii wo tar twika nuwam fichangero tiye na dige bulangko toke. chiki ma nangen yirum dige kakuloko dii kwama. na wo kwama ma Musa nin biweret, fiya cho chwiti na cho mũũ bikure: toõ, kwama yii ki, “ma diger dong-dong na wo chi merang mwen dor bang-ngereu.”
di la nangen do Almachiya yowe la wo chiye gwam. wori cho nii tebere yortum norem, woro chi takum na yortum norem boche.

di la wo cho nor miro wo ma ti ka-nge loh Israila, bwiko kume niwo, nuwa Teluwe, ma yoti bolang miko nyii chi, na mulanti mor nere chiye mani yilam kwama chinen, chi kene chiyan yilam nob mib.

bwiko ywellum dige wori, nob wabeb bikurebo, ki do, dokuwe bikulro nine kir-kir chi ma nangen chiyeroti.

chari kange dige noka mwere kange chika nirbanka kidemen-kidemen, wori dige yo a manangti, nime na bidoti yorangi.

kebo ki bwiyal nibe kange nenne di la ki bwiyale che, cho do'o fiye wuchake kiriti win chwat na nobo gwame che, yo'o binen fanka wo dire.
tano bwiyal nibe Kane nenne, ka-nge te'eka dor nobo ka-ngum wuchake chiye, nir chiti, ka-nge bwii chiye.
Tenkang bwiyale Almachiya wo bo fiye yuwa tangbeko wuchake bak-ni-bak neken dor chero twika ficha-nger, kwama wo nir nerberoti fiye nange do yorbo bwiyam bwiya na bo wab kwama nii dume.
cho dige bwiye, Almachiya cho fiye wab kanka noro fwiko, wuro bwi nyo, ma bwaro wo chokkum nobo dimer noro chare, ker bwirangke chi, wuro kwama cho na yo'o nor kwali chi bak-ni-bak.

Almachiya dobo fiye wuchak chi mũũ ki ka-nge, wuro betenkar dige wo na bilengke che. nyo chon ya mor dii kwama ki dorcer, nimde cho ya kabum kwama ker ber.

tano nyori tamyo cha nuwa dotange kiriti-kiriti fiye kabak dor bitiner, di na weu kiriti win chi fwetanche, chwile kalewo nin na tum bwirangke, cho chwi cho nẽẽ ken gor chere.
nawo chi binen gwam bo bwiya kiriti win chwat, bwiko chek, kum kan bolang.
nyo Almachiya wo chi nẽẽ kiriti win chwat, be na cho tum bwrangke nobo kila, yila na yobe che kebo nangen tũũka bwirangke, di la dor nobo wuro nintang choti ki birum nẽẽ na fuloci.
nyori warfundo nyrom dike yoryore a boutiye kebo yirombo chuwo ki bwichi nobbo ya'ati kwama nine mani a yila nobti kambo ken ki ker twika wo nob twika mati chor kange chore.
na wo nyori twika nuwangeko datenbo a timka? wori chwi ninin nob wabkako chim nirum chi kiritti wiin, chi nyombo bwirang kere.
la twirangka nuwangek yilam diker kwaka ker bwirang keret chor kange chor.
la bwiyale kwama kange nibe mani a tum bwirang kere ti.
fiya kiritti bou dor bitinere chon tokki, twika nuwangek kange neka luma kebo dike kom chitiye, lan bwiyo ka ywel mene,
twika kange meka dor bwiangge kebo diker luma kime.
la min tokki, “to'o min wo, na wo mulangum dor mir mor bifumere, nan ma dike mo chwitiye.”'
ki ka'aba cho tokki “kebo twika nuwangek, kebo luma, kebo twika dor bwirang keret kom chitiye kaka kebo diker kom nuwa luma chek tiye” wuro twika nuwangeko chi mati mor werfune.
la chon tokki, “to'o min wo nan ma dike mo chitiye” cho tum dikero mati ki ka'aba na cho bou chi ki a mati na yobbe cheu.
wuro chin nirum wuchak mor neka bwiye Yeesu kiritti, kiritti wiin na yilam na gwamme che.
kume bwiko kume nob twika nuwangek tim ma kwama nin nangen ti. cho ne twikako chuwo kir-kir, twika nuwangeko wuro twibo bwirang keret wiye.
la kiritti ne twika nuwangek kiritti wiin na wo gwam me, cho yiiken kang ko chartiyere kwama.
cho ki nin tangi na nob kiyeb chebo yilam fiye fuwa na'a chek.
ki twika nuwangek wiin, chon ywel nobbo chi nirum wuchake yilam dikero ken kambo ken, diiri.
takeu, yuwatangbeko wuchakeu war binen ker. ki ka'aba chon tokki,

channeu, no tubka dike buro no wiri, nuwangek bweirang kere mani.
nyori ker mibo biki bikwan neret bandoken fiye wuchake ki bwiyale Yeesu.
wuro cho nure fwirko nyiime che cha wom binene mor kyelange, wuro dangi bwichi.
wori biki nii twiika nuwangek dur lo kwama.
nyori bi kutauten bidom ki nere ken, won chiyako dim diye na bilengke che, wori ner bero chin tem manki duti kwaka dikero bwir, bwi beu chin nirum ki mwembo manki dutiye.
bitam kibi kwan warka nyo nere be, wori nii wo ma norrou wi ki bilengke.
bi to'o nure wo ba nekang kuru ti cwikangka kange maka dikero kenne.
bi yilotende mwerkangka beko nawo kangum bo maneu. bi nekang buti bikwang neret kir-kir na wo kom to'o kakuko chuwo dadome.
no bo ma bwirang kiritti ki nyomka bwikoba yuwa nyomka bilengke, nuwangek bwirang kere mani tak.
nyori kan taito dur bolangere kange kirako chilong-chiloge wo twinob kiyeb kwama.
nii wo ko werfun Musaro di chan bwiya cii duwe mani dorwarka nobbo yob kaka ta'ar.

wori bon nyimom wuro yii ki, ya'aka chunero na mi, man ya'am chunero chuwo takau kwama a ma warka nobbo locheu.
diker tayer na yarken kang kwama ki dume;
la kwa ki kumeni chumeu, bwiko ka yuwo nyomka, la kom mwirumum doka cherka dotange dure.
kom fiya kwenduwe mor nobbo ki bi torr kange dotange, kom nuwa dotange ti na wo kangumbo do'o more che kene.
wori kom bunang nobbo fuchinabbo kom chiya ki fwor neret kulen kimero chi yuwome. kom nyomom ki bwikimi kom wi ki kulendo wo yoryori bak-ni-bak.
nyori kom mirang de bikwang neret ki mero wi, wuro wiki ya'aka ko dur.
kom cwi mwirumka ti, na yiolam no kom dikero kwama cwitiyeri, kan yuwo norro cho ma bineneu.
ki kini bi duwar, nii wo bou tiye “bichuwom an bou mani a ma fiyeti.
mimbo wuchakeu an fulo ki bilen kere. nocho yilaken ki bwimri mani ma nuwa lumati kange cho.
la bo mani mor nobbo wuro yilaken ki bwim fiye twalangka, la boh wi more buro ki bilengke.
bilengke co ciya kako ki dike bro bo yo neer dor cireu. co ciya kako ki dike nuwe tobeu.
ki ciro co tenkwanib bebo fiya ciyaka fiye kwama wiye.
ki bilengke ba nyumom kalewo kwama fwel ki ker cer, wori dike brombo to ti ki nuweu fwelu bo dike to ti ki nuweu.
ki bilengke Habila ne kwama chikako ficange la kayinu ceu, wo kwama ciya cinen con ni bilengke. kwama toki yora dor luma cero ca neu, ki bilengke Habila tok kere bwentano con bwiyameu.

co ki ton kaba cinan loro ki kwar kureuwo nii yabi kange mukako kwama.

Biru bwe tomange Yecu fabubo wo kwama coki watanum watange Buntu, galatiya kaya dki ya aciya kange bitiiya.
Wo ki nyomka kwama teu kange yuwa tangbek kwama wo nii nirkau kange lomjome kange cor ka bwieyalek Yecu Kritti luma a fiya nen filang mweko ayukten.
Bibwiyer ano kwamanin Te cer Yecu Kritti ki cini ceu tenang tenangeu, co ca nebo fwir na yim yonerimbo ki dumeu ki kwenka Yecuk bwar.

co ni fanko mur bwiranka be, kebe kabe ki kwace, la kange dor bitine roce gwam.
la nyeu co ma nyumom la bon nyumomco na bo bwang ten werfuner cerori.
nii wo ki con “nyumom kwama,” la bwangten bo werfuner cereri nii cwerke bilenkero mani wercer.

na nii wo ki co ki no mor kwamari, tam ca yam bo wo Yeecu Almacifu yau.

ma mulan kumen wo kom bi beyo lomi ma cwi-cwiyeu wo ni cin cutam kumen bwiran ke kume wi ker denece.
man mulang kumen tebbo, wori kom nyumom co, wuro wi tun ki kabau. man mulang kumen kom bi bei bayolobeu wori kom wi kibi kwan la ker kwamaro yimwi more kume, wokom cam turani kange bwerko. man mulan kumen bi be yo, wori kom nyumom teeu.
man mulan kumen tebbo, wori kom nyumom co won wi fiya ki kabau, man mulang kumen bi bei ba yilo bei wori kom wi kibi kwan la ker kwamaro yim more kume, la kom cam turani ki bwirko
ko cwire kalewo, kaka dike mor kalewo, no na kange cwi kale wori cwika teeka mani more ce.

Yahuza canga Yeesu Alamasiya, take yi Yakubu, fiye nubo co cowe wiye, Nubo ma cwiye mor kwama Tee cokumcoke na Yeesu Kristi ce.
Cireduwe, kange daka neret kange cwika a bwii fiye kumenen.
Nubo ma cwiye mi ma nyi bi kwane na mulang kumen ki ker fuloka beko gwam, tam makumen biweret kambo dor bilenker wo ci ne nubo bwantenco tiye Krisiti win cwar yokka man.
Di kange nubo curab dou ki dang yurangum yurange, wuro ci mulangi dor warke ciye fiya ki kutanka con man ki bilenker, wuro folongum luma kwama kange kayaka, take cin kanangum nii wine, dur kange Teluwebe, Yeesu Almasiya.
Mi cwiti nan bulang kumen bwen duwale kweri kom nyomom dikeco, ki yika kwama fulo nubokangem beten masare, di ki bwi con twallangum nubo nebo bilenke.
nob. tomange ce wucakke wuro tabo dur bikwan ciyere di cin dubom fiye ciye kwattiye, kwama bwelmaro diri mor kumtacile fir nimde kakuko durko, wo bolange ce.
Ci nyo na saduma kange Gomarata, kange bertinimbo kentangum kange ciyeu wuro neken dor ciyero kayaka, ci bwangten dilankakoti wo kebo wo daten. di cin yilam diker danke wuro ci nuwa kira manki dika.
Nyo nob dukumenbo wuro ci kan bwiciye ti, ci cwekan liyab boti take ci tok dikeroti dor wo na duktangkakoce.
Di bwen nob tomangebo wucake, dur nob tomangebbo wucake fiya co kwobkanti kange kwalkanka kange bwekelkele dor bilen Musa, letankbo tokka kero kange na warka ko ce dor cer. Nyo co yi ki Di Teluwe a kwenang mwenteng.
Di nubo wuro boti ki kunka dor ci nyombe gwam. nubo wuro wiki mulen biyuwaret, ci kwob dorcero nen buwar.
Kwanci wari cin bwangten nure kayinu, take cin yarken mor letanka bal'amu ki na ci fiya mwem cin bwiyam mor funere nawo kora ceu.
Wuro naba yurangum yurange mor cika kume na cwikace cin nuwa ti ka luma kwenduwe man, tai man. Ka dor cir ci catiye ki kwaci, Ci biloro wo mani bo ki mweme wo yuwako ywa cotiye. cin tini tirangum bitutti man, bilentini kiriti yob, kwomkwobe fiya nintini nin.
cin mwelangka mwemek wima wo ki ki bibutetwele, ci kwilangti mor funi kwenduwe ciye. Ciki no nabitirendo certiye wuro ci tank kumtacili fi kiriti kiriti diri diri.
Ahnuhu nii na nibere ce teu Adamu nin ma dukume ddor ciyer ki, To Teluwe an boki nob cebo wucakke bikatentini.
Co warum ki warka dor nubo gwam, ya mwa nubo mani nuware mor nangen ciyer na bongtu wo ci mani nure wo datenbe kange keti wo cilongi wo nob bwirangke tokangi dor cere.
Burombo ci yiti toki kom toke, nob fwennab, wuro bwangten dilanka ciyekoti na cile ce, burombo ma nyalti ki kwilanka, nob wambirub na fiya ka ciyeko.
Di la kom nubo ma cwiye kom bulangi, kange ketito wo nob tomange Yeesu Almasiya be ci yi kom nanduwo.
Cin yi kom ki, “Mor kume ni cwile, an fiya nob mwankerebo wuro bwanten dilangka ciyekoti na bwini wabe.
Nubo wuro nob boti ki yalkangka, takeu, ci bibei dorbitiner, ci man ki yuwa tangbeko wucakke.
Di la kom nubo ma cwiye, kom mu dor kumero nen bilenker la gwamme kom na bwayilence, take kom kwob diloti mor yuwa tangbeko wucakke.
Kom tam dor kumero mor cwika kwama, tak kom nintang cireduwe teluwe yeesu Almasiya wo boti ki dume diriye.
Kom nung cireduwe fiye nubo wo nyomantiye nin. Kom fulo kangembo kira ki cwabrika.
Nubo kange kom nung cinen cireduwe ki yila bwik, kom nung yai ka bwen kulendo bwiciyeri.
Nawo fiye woki bikwan na ywamkom kottangka, co dok kom ti kom ti kambu duktanka bokaceko man ki duti kange bilanktumbo tenan tenange.
Fiye kwama wine nii fulokabe fiye Yeesu Almasiya Teluwe, duktangka, dur kange liyar kange bikwan a no nimde fiyang gwam, nawo kange diri, A ti nyo.

yiki, inudang dika mwa toweu mor bifumeve, natumg lowabe kwaamaro niber Afisu, wo simirns, wo Birgamas, wo Tayatira, wo sardisu, wo filadalfiya, kange wo laudiku'ya.”
min yila nan nuwa dirowo yiye kero tiyui, mi yilari laminto talkir niber dor diker timer cer.

Nii tomange tenangtenange tu tero cerkar ter kuwaska nerek, merkenco mor moremme titoki ki, “kinco nurewo, babila, linalorodur an merkenco bitine kibi kwan, mani atotencotiak.
Dir nubero kwabibentiyeu, nuboka nuwetiyeu, nubocu liranktiyeu, kange nubo biro cu.............. mani anuwsten ciiti more cetak. Unw ango kange mani kange twari................... wo afiys morece mari anuws dirr kuwaaka nevekti wi morecetak.
Filang takiretko mari cwobten reka filangekti morece. mari anuwa dir nii birnerti kange binne morece, inwori............ incii bábei nubo ma liyan dorbitinerotiye, mor.................... mwa bolnubo take.
Morece ciifiya buyal wobtomangeb dukumebe kange nubo ne bilenke, kange buyal nubo ciitwd dorbitinere gwari.”
Bwiko dike tinim buro ri man nuwa diro kange wo cerkang dir nubo ducce dii kwama cii tok ti ki, “halliluya, fuloka duk tangka, kange bikwan na kwama be ce.
Warke ceu bilenke ri cwika duwe mani, wori cin warker nawiye dor burotume durko wo kangum dor bitiner ro ki burotum cem me. Cin yam nando co ki bwiyale canga tini ce wo co nanwiye ki burotume coreu.
Ciin tok ker owo yobe ceu. Haliluya yilombo ceru cinen bak-nin bak.
Nubo dur tinimbo cilombo naareu kange dikero wo ci fweli ki dume naareu ciin yarken bitine cii wab kwama, wo yim dor kutile liyareu. Cii tok ti ki “Ati nyo, Halliluya!”
La diro ceru kutile liyare nin tok ti ki “Caklang kwama be, kom canga tinni ce gwam, kom nubo ko cwa tiye, nubo ki bi bikwan lkiyare kange wo man ki kibi bikwan liyareu,”.
La man nuwa diker na dor nober ducce, na diir cuka mwenger na diir kume tak, tok ti ki “halliluya!” Teluwe maliyar ti, kwama be nii bi kwane gwamme.
Bi ma bititen, bi ne co dur, tak ri bi ne co duktangka wori cika naka be kwame ko nin buu ri nawiye bineu ywelum bwiceu.
Ciin dub co naci dum bwiceu ki kwilendo ki filang kange wo lalang merek koceu yora dutti maniyeu (wori lalang mereko kendo twiya twiyau ki nung cak-cake nangen nob kwama ko wucakke).
Nii tomange wucakke yiye ki “Mulangum wi nob bi bwiyere be buro fiya bicuuwor naci ya fiye cika naka be kwamake.” Cin yiye tak ki, “Mulangum wuro” buro bilenke ti kwama ko.
man yari man canga ken kange mo, kange keb mwebburo tam warke dor Yeesu. ko wab kwama, wori warke dor Yeesu re be warke yuwa tangbe ker dukumer”.
Di la mato dii kwama wumom la ma tok ri mato tuwa fuworko. Cii ki cuwo nii wo yim dor cereu ki nii ci ciya cike kange bilenke. Cike ma warke mor cak-cake ci ma kwenti.
Nuwe ceu kino na biyen kirer la con wiki lalang duwek ducce dorcer. cin wiki den mulangum cinen wo no kebo cori kange nii man wo nyome.
Ci dum ki belle wo cii dokken mor bwiyale. La den cero ki cuwo ti kii ker kwamak.
Nob kwenebo dii kwamau bwang cinen tenti dor tuwa fuwor tini, cii dum ki kwilen lalang merek ko twiya twiyau wo fuwoce ri manki duti takeu.
Mor nyire ce kulendo nyiyo cacau ceuti wo cii torang nubo kumtacilleti cikeu ri can ma liyar cer ki dang kiyemerek. ci fuwarang fiya cokka mweb Inabi ti ki dotange funer kwama nii bikwane gwamme.
Cin wiki den mulangum bellece nen kange ki co “Liya Liyabbe, teluwe, teluwe tini”.
Man to bwe tomange wuccake tim kakuk. Ci cuwo bi cuwor tikidiro dur fiye bilibetini cuto dor re “ko bou, ko mweri wari caka cika ko dur kwama ce.
Ko bou ko no wo nang liyatini nang nubo ne bi weret tiye, nang nubo dure, nang tuwa tini kange nubo kwob ci tiye kange nang nubo gwam, wo ki cerka kange cangabbo nubo kwanneu kange buro man kibi kwanneu.
Man to durtini liyatinimbo dor bitineu kange nob kweneb cebo. Ciki mweri naci te kwen kange wo dor tuware kange nob kweneb ceko.
Cin tam liya dor bitinere durko kange nob tomangeb dukumer cwerke wo merang diker nyimanka ti kaceu. Ki diker nyimangka tini buro cin bolang buro yom yirom biciro wo kange buro ma tati bak-bakeu
Ciin twallangum tangnim cem bo ki kulen do ceru nyi nii wo dor tuwereu. Bilibeu gwam-gwam carangum bilentini ceu.
La min to ni nagen kwama yirauti firen di kwama, wiki diker kang cek.
La ci too no cwe charko wuro cho bwekelkele bwamco coro kwini bikate.
Ciin merken co mor buwakke wo manki dikau nung. co kwati dur liyar cerwi dor cer. Nyo na wo kariyilo ci bolangten nubo nyombo ker kwamaere wo adimti coro lam bikate. bwiko wo di tam nyo a nyamkang cimen bi duwar.
La wi man too fitiyimken nubo wuro yim dor cereu chi nubo chi neci bi kwan bolange. Lami to dume nubowo chi mwatang doreu ki ker Yeesu kang ker kwamar. Ci wabo bicirin kange diro cerkangce, chin ko ywoaka cerkangka tikob ci kang kangcik cin fulongum yim cimbo, cin ca liyar kange bibwekwama coro lam bikate.
Tang ni nubo bwiyameu, yilaubo ki dume, no coro bikate dimeri na yimde. Wuro co kwenka nubo bwiyameu ki kaba.
Nii wo fiya calangka wucakeu, co nii wo ki tureni mor kwenka nubo ki kaba. buro wo yobe mani ki bikwan dor nubo wuro. Ciya yilam nubo wab kwama kange bibwe kwama ciya yi liyar kange co ki coro bi kate.
Lano coro bikate lamdi, ciya cikom bwekelkele furcuna.
Can cerken kale na co bolang nubo ti wo nyumbo ker kwamareu, kung nari kalewe Gog kange magog mweranci na kwenece kilatum cembo dong dong kange biyabombo caji yeu.
Cin yati kale wuro ni cin kangtangum fiye nubo ne bilenke wiyeu ci yimwe. La kirako yirau di kwama twirang ci.
Bwekelkele wo bolcitiyeu merken co mor kire wo furko cabie, fiye ci merum nange nicwerke ni wabka ciya nuwa dotange kume kange kakuk bak-ni-bak.
Lami to dikero dor ko kange nubo yim dorcere. kalewo kange di kwama cin cwam tikobcem, la cin manki fiye ciya yakentiye.
Min to nubo kwarangum me nubo dur kange bibei ci tirangum wi kabum na gwomfe la cin wo bifimtini. la ci wom bifimer dumero. Bilendo an macimen bolang ki diker mulangum mor takarau, ki dikero ci maneu.
Wima nubo wanang mureceu. Bwararo kange lo bibwetinim, nubo bwangten mbwanang mureceu ci macimen bolang dong dong kange diker ci maneu.
La ci merken wuro kang lobibwiti kira. Wuro co bwaro wo yobbe bitike Kira.
Kwarub niwo ci fibo dencer mulang mulange mor bifumer dumeri, can merken co kira.
La min to dii kwam fwir kange dorbitinero fwir, wori dii kwama wo ki ƙabau kange dorbitiner ƙabako cum, kange wima mani.
Min to cinan loro wucakeu, Urusalima fwirko, wo yirau dii kwama Kwama nin, ywelum ywele na bine ci manten bwayilen ker nina bare cereu.
Min diro dur dor kutile liyare tok ti ki, “To! fiye yime Kwamau kino wari kange nubo fir tini, tak keu ca yi kange cii. Cii an yilam nubo loce, la Kwama ki bwico an yi kange cii, can yilam Kwama ciye.
Can wam mwem nuwem ciyembo wiyak nuwe ciye, bwaro mani a kumti tak, kakaa fir neret, kakaa wiye, kakaa dotange. Dikerro car ko cum.
Co nii wo ci yim dor kutile liyareu yiki,” To! mi yilam ki dikero kwarub fwice.” Con tiki, “Mulangum wuro wori ketito buro daten ciyaka kange bilenke.”
Cin yiye ciki, “Dike buro dim! Min alpha kange omega, terka kange dika ki niwo nuwa dilo mwe tiyeu man nee co noka ki lime nek fiye mwem dumem bo ceruw tiyeu.
Nii wo fiya tureniye ri atin ye kwali dikero buro, la man yilam Kwama ce, co can yilam bibwe mi.
Dila nubo buro tārangi nyeu, nob bwini bilenkeb, nnubo ma dikero ti yei nyeu, nubo twal dortiyeu, nubo ma bwiratum tiyeu, nub buwabbebo, nubo wab fulen tiyeu, kange nob cwerke bo gwam, fiye yime ceu an yila mor kirako diriye. Cuwo bwaro yobeu.
Wiin mor bibei tomange diikwama nibereu bou mi nen, wo ki kwellini niber dim ki fencangê bwiko nibereu, yiki, “Bou fo. man nang mwen bineu fwirko, Bibwe Kwama
La cin tuye mor yuwa tangba cu ki mo bangko durko cwemi nye ri cin dang mencinan loro wucakke Urchalima ceru dii Kwama yirauti fiye Kwama nine.
Uruchalima wiki duktongka Kwamak, wo mim langka ceko kino na bicuka bwayilenne, na terro tiblangti tiblange- wo ki filang na ter dacenner.
Cin wi ki tiyakko duwi duwe, ki nyilotini kwob cilom bo yob, ki nob tomangebo dii kwamau kwob cilombo yob nyilotini ko nin. Dor nyilo tini cin mulangti tuwe loni kwob cilombo yob wo bibei Icraila ciyeu.
Cungako twareu nyiloko wi ta'ar, bangkonin nyiloko ta'ar kwacalmen nyiloko wi ta'ar.
Tiyak cinan loro wiki kwar mukaro kwob cilombo yob, wi dor ciyer takeu dentini nob tomangeb wo Be Kwame Kwama ko kwob cilom bo yobbe.
Co nii wo tokker kange meu, wiki dang mwin nek naci cuwam cinanloro, nyilo ceko kange tiyak ceko.
Cinanloro ci muweu, cuwemtum cembo kino donki donki kange, kwiyatum cembo. Cin cuwam cinanloro ki dank cuwakam, bikateu kwob cilombo yob ki cwemer (Cunga ceko, kwiyatum cembo, kange cwemtum cembo dongi dongi)
Cin cuwam ten tiyak ceko tak, tu tum cembo nako 475.2 ki cuwaka nifirek.( Wo co cuwaka bibei tomange Kwama ko dii kwamau).
Tiyakko cii muki jaspa, la cinanloro ka den mwiner, wo twelum na nuwe turome.
Kwar tiyak kero cin man ten bwayilen ki tero ken. Wo ki kabau jaspa, yobe ceu saffir, taare ceu agat, naare ceu emaral
nunge ceu onis, nukkune ceucardiyus, nibere ceu kimsolat, wo naurube ceu beril, wo teere ceu tofaz, kwobbe ceukirisofaras, wo kwob cilombo wiinee ceu yakinta, kwobcilombo yobe ceu ametis.
Nyiloko kwob cilombo yob beu co kwilen bwayilenero kwob cilombo yobeu; nyilo ki wiin wiine ci ywelang ki kwilen bwayilenero wiin wiin. nur le tini mor cinan loro nineu ci ywilang ki den mwinner na nuwee turome yanglangeu.
Mi tobo bikur waber wi mor cinar loro nin, wori Teeluwe nii bikwane gwam kange Bekwameu cii bikur waber cero.
Cinan loro dobo kakuk kakaa cwiyako na ne filang cinen wori duktangka Kwama ko ne filang koti cinen, la tal kira ceu co Bekwameu.
Nubo kumtaciliu atin ya-yam mor filang cinanlore ko co. Liyatini dor bitinereu atin borangu ki yora ciyeko more ce.
Nyilo tini ceu mani a nung ti ki kakuk, takkeu, kume mani wi.
Ci an bouki yorak kange neka durek nubo kumta ciliu more ce.
La dike kange man wo ki duti yeu a doti more ce. Gwam nii wo ma dike kange ti wo kwenduwe ceu kakaa ki cwerke a dotiye, dila ka nubo buro den ciyero mulangum mor diker mulangkar dumek Bekwame ke.
la bibwe tomange wucake, nang men caji mwem dumem wo manki dutiye. ceruti kutile liyar kwama ka-nge be kwameceu
tiber dor nurero cinar lore. bwatiye dume wi kongeni caji nin, wo ne bituti ti wangko kwob culombo yob mor cwiyake. lallu tiye ceu na twaka nobbeko bitentine.
ciilka mani tak. kutile liyar kwama ka-nge be kwame ceu, a nowi cinnar loro nin, cangab cebo an ma nangen cangabero.
ci an to'o tikob cebo, den cero an no'o tikob cib.
kume ka-nge man tak, mani ciya do'o filang tal kiristi kaka filang kakuker, wori Teluwe kwama an wen cinen. ci an ca liyar bak-ni-bak.
bwe tomange wucake yii ye, “kero buro ciyam-ciyam cuko, bilengke tak. Teluwe, kwama yuwa tangbe nob dukume, tom nii tomange ce wucake na nung cangab cebo nin dige a bwiti kutangbe.”
“To'o, mi bouti kutangbo, nii bibwiyere wo tam ker dukumer bifumero weu.”
mo yuwana, mo ma nuwa, to'o digero weu. fiya cuwo ma nuwa ma to'o ciyau, min yarken kabum nani bibwe tomange wucake wo nangkan men citiyeu.
la con yii mare nyo, min nii bwanka na mo, ka-nge yitub mweb nob dukumeb ka-nge buro ne bilengke kero wuro mor bifure wo. “wab kwama;”
yii ye, cumom de ketito, wori kini dadom
wuri manki cakcaka a ca kaba manki cakcake, nii wo ki dutiye, a ca kaba ki fitongka bwiyek cek. nii wo ki cakcake a ca kaba ki cakcake ce. nii wo wucake a kaba ki wucake ce”
“To'o mi bouti kutangbo, ya'aka miko wi kang mik, man ya'a nobo gwam dong-dong ka-nge nangendo ci maneu.
Mo Alpha ka-nge Omega, kaba ka-nge cwile, terka dige ka-nge cwile ce.
Nob bibwiyer nobbo nirum belle ciye na fiya ciyaka na ci ca bwatiye dume, takeu na ci doken cinnar lor nyiilo cek.
kaleu, bicwetini, nob buwab, nob fuleneb, nob kayatum, nob twalkab, ka-nge nobo gwam wo bilang maka digero bwir tiye.
mo Yeesu, min tomu bwe tomange wucake na ne kom warke dige buro na nob bwangka kwama. mo dimer na niya Dauda bitiner burit wo flange.
yuwa tangbe ka-nge bine cin tokki, “bou” wuro nuwari a toki ak-nge ki, “bou” nii wo nuwa dulomwe tiye ka-nge nii wo cwitiye ca bou na ci fiya mwem dumem luma.
mi yii nobbo gwam wo nuwa keti dukume bifumere: no ka-nge yokten dor cer di, kwama an yok cinenten finjange mor bifumero weu.
No ka-nge kwom wi mor ketito wo bifumer dukumereri, kwama an kwob cinen mor tii dume, mor cinar lor wucake, wuro ci mulangi mor bifumere weu.
